<script>
// ===== STATE =====
let state = {
  airPath: 'supply',
  material: 'metal',
  shape: 'round',
  ductSegment: 'trunk',
  dialParam: 'cfm',
  isDragging: false,
  velocity: 0,
  friction: 0,
  cfm: 400
};

// ===== CONSTANTS =====
// ACCA Manual D Table 3-1 — Maximum Duct Velocities (FPM)
const MANUAL_D_VELOCITY = {
  supply: {
    rigid:  { trunk: 900, branch: 900, runout: 700 },
    flex:   { trunk: 700, branch: 700, runout: 700 }
  },
  return: {
    rigid:  { trunk: 700, branch: 700, runout: 500 },
    flex:   { trunk: 700, branch: 700, runout: 500 }
  },
  recommended: {
    supply: { rigid: { trunk: 700, branch: 600, runout: 0 }, flex: { trunk: 600, branch: 600, runout: 600 } },
    return: { rigid: { trunk: 600, branch: 400, runout: 0 }, flex: { trunk: 600, branch: 400, runout: 0 } }
  },
  filterGrille: 300,
  returnGrille: 500
};
// Helper: get max velocity for current calc tab (uses trunk as default for forward calc)
function getMaxVelocity(airPath, material, ductSegment) {
  var mat = (material === 'flex') ? 'flex' : 'rigid';
  var seg = ductSegment || 'trunk';
  var path = airPath || 'supply';
  try { return MANUAL_D_VELOCITY[path][mat][seg]; } catch(e) { return 700; }
}
// Legacy compat
const MAX_VELOCITY = { supply: 900, return: 700 };
const MAX_FRICTION = 0.08;

// ===== CORE PHYSICS (ACCA Manual D / Swamee-Jain) =====
function frictionFactor(D_ft, V_fps, roughness) {
  const Re = V_fps * D_ft / (1.63e-4);
  if (Re < 100) return 0.08;
  const term1 = roughness / (3.7 * D_ft);
  const term2 = 5.74 / Math.pow(Re, 0.9);
  return 0.25 / Math.pow(Math.log10(term1 + term2), 2);
}

function getRoughness(mat, insulated) {
  // Roughness in feet: metal=0.0003, metalLined=0.003, flex=0.003, flexLined=0.005
  if (mat === 'metal') return insulated ? 0.003 : 0.0003;
  return insulated ? 0.005 : 0.003;
}

function frictionLoss(D_in, cfm, matOverride, insOverride) {
  // Returns friction loss in IWC per 100ft for round duct
  const D_ft = D_in / 12;
  const A = Math.PI * Math.pow(D_ft / 2, 2);
  const V = cfm / A; // FPM
  if (V < 1) return 0;
  const V_fps = V / 60;
  const rho = 0.075;
  const mat = matOverride || state.material || 'metal';
  const insEl = document.getElementById('insulatedToggle');
  const ins = (insOverride !== undefined) ? insOverride : (insEl ? insEl.checked : false);
  const rough = getRoughness(mat, ins);
  const f = frictionFactor(D_ft, V_fps, rough);
  return f * (100 / D_ft) * (rho * V_fps * V_fps) / (2 * 32.174) / 5.192;
}

function flexFactor(compression) {
  if (compression === 0) return 1;
  if (compression <= 15) return 1 + (compression / 15);
  return 2 + ((compression - 15) / 15) * 2;
}

function rectEquivDiameter(w, h) {
  return 1.3 * Math.pow(w * h, 0.625) / Math.pow(w + h, 0.25);
}

// ===== PAGE NAVIGATION =====
function showPage(key) {
  const map = { 'roomcfm': 0, 'calculator': 1, 'eqlen': 2, 'system': 3, 'frworksheet': 4, 'filters': 5, 'psychro': 6 };
  const idx = map[key] ?? 0;
  document.querySelectorAll('.page').forEach((p, i) => {
    p.classList.toggle('active', i === idx);
  });
  document.querySelectorAll('.nav-tab[data-page]').forEach(btn => {
    btn.classList.toggle('active', btn.dataset.page === key);
  });
}

// ===== CALCULATOR CONTROLS =====
// setDialParam removed (dial removed)

function setAirPath(val) {
  state.airPath = val;
  document.querySelectorAll('#airPathControl [data-airpath]').forEach(b => {
    b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.airpath === val);
  });
  updateCalcFilterVisibility();
  calculate();
}

function setMaterial(val) {
  state.material = val;
  document.querySelectorAll('#materialControl [data-material]').forEach(b => {
    b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.material === val);
  });
  const comp = document.getElementById('compressionSection');
  if (comp) comp.style.display = val === 'flex' ? 'block' : 'none';
  calculate();
}

function setShape(val) {
  state.shape = val;
  document.querySelectorAll('#shapeControl [data-shape]').forEach(b => {
    b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.shape === val);
  });
  const rg = document.getElementById('roundSizeGroup');
  const wg = document.getElementById('rectWGroup');
  if (rg) rg.style.display = val === 'round' ? '' : 'none';
  if (wg) wg.style.display = val === 'rect' ? '' : 'none';
  calculate();
}

function setDuctSegment(val) {
  state.ductSegment = val;
  document.querySelectorAll('#segmentControl [data-segment]').forEach(b => {
    b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.segment === val);
  });
  calculate();
}

function updateCompression() {
  const slider = document.getElementById('compressionSlider');
  if (!slider) return;
  const c = parseInt(slider.value) || 4;
  const valEl = document.getElementById('compressionValue');
  if (valEl) valEl.textContent = c + '%';
  const compInput = document.getElementById('compressionInput');
  if (compInput && compInput !== document.activeElement) compInput.value = c;
  document.querySelectorAll('.compression-presets [data-compression]').forEach(b => {
    b.classList.toggle('active', parseInt(b.dataset.compression) === c);
  });
  const impact = document.getElementById('compressionImpact');
  if (impact) {
    const fct = flexFactor(c);
    if (c <= 10) { impact.textContent = c + '% compressed \u2014 ' + fct.toFixed(1) + 'x friction'; impact.className = 'compression-impact low'; }
    else if (c <= 20) { impact.textContent = c + '% compressed \u2014 ' + fct.toFixed(1) + 'x friction'; impact.className = 'compression-impact medium'; }
    else { impact.textContent = c + '% compressed \u2014 ' + fct.toFixed(1) + 'x friction \u26a0 HIGH'; impact.className = 'compression-impact high'; }
  }
  calculate();
}

function setCompression(pct) {
  const slider = document.getElementById('compressionSlider');
  if (slider) { slider.value = pct; updateCompression(); }
}

// ===== MAIN CALCULATOR =====
function calculate() {
  const cfmInput = document.getElementById('cfmInput');
  if (!cfmInput) return;

  const cfm = parseFloat(cfmInput.value) || 0;
  let D_in;

  if (state.shape === 'round') {
    const sel = document.getElementById('roundSizeVal');
    D_in = parseFloat(sel ? sel.value : 10);
  } else {
    const w = parseFloat((document.getElementById('rectWVal') || {}).value || 10);
    const h = parseFloat((document.getElementById('rectHVal') || {}).value || 8);
    D_in = rectEquivDiameter(w, h);
  }

  const D_ft = D_in / 12;
  const A = Math.PI * Math.pow(D_ft / 2, 2);
  const velocity = cfm > 0 ? cfm / A : 0;

  let friction = 0;
  if (cfm > 0 && D_in > 0) {
    friction = frictionLoss(D_in, cfm);
    if (state.material === 'flex') {
      const comp = parseInt((document.getElementById('compressionSlider') || {}).value || 0);
      friction *= flexFactor(comp);
    }
  }

  // Suggested duct size (find smallest round duct that keeps vel & friction in limits)
  const maxV = getMaxVelocity(state.airPath, state.material, state.ductSegment);
  const sizes = [4,5,6,7,8,9,10,12,14,16,18,20,22,24];
  let sugSize = sizes[sizes.length - 1];
  for (const sz of sizes) {
    const sD = sz / 12;
    const sA = Math.PI * Math.pow(sD / 2, 2);
    const sV = cfm > 0 ? cfm / sA : 0;
    let sFR = cfm > 0 ? frictionLoss(sz, cfm) : 0;
    if (state.material === 'flex') {
      const comp = parseInt((document.getElementById('compressionSlider') || {}).value || 0);
      sFR *= flexFactor(comp);
    }
    if (sV <= maxV && sFR <= MAX_FRICTION) { sugSize = sz; break; }
  }

  // Max TEL at 0.08 IWC: maxTEL = ASP / frictionRate * 100
  // Using the user's friction input as ASP proxy
  const frInput = document.getElementById('frictionInput');
  const frVal = parseFloat(frInput ? frInput.value : 0.06) || 0;
  const maxTEL = friction > 0 ? (frVal / friction) * 100 : 0;

  // Max CFM this duct can carry at 0.08 IWC/100ft (accounting for compression)
  let maxCFMforDuct = 0;
  if (D_in > 0) {
    let lo = 10, hi = maxV * A; // velocity-capped upper bound
    for (let it = 0; it < 50; it++) {
      let mid = (lo + hi) / 2;
      let testFR = frictionLoss(D_in, mid);
      if (state.material === 'flex') {
        const comp2 = parseInt((document.getElementById('compressionSlider') || {}).value || 0);
        testFR *= flexFactor(comp2);
      }
      if (testFR <= MAX_FRICTION) { maxCFMforDuct = mid; lo = mid; }
      else { hi = mid; }
      if (hi - lo < 0.5) break;
    }
    // Also cap by velocity
    const maxCFMvel = maxV * A;
    if (maxCFMforDuct > maxCFMvel) maxCFMforDuct = maxCFMvel;
  }

  // Store on state for header pills
  state.velocity = velocity;
  state.friction = friction;
  state.cfm = cfm;

  // Update result cards
  const e = id => document.getElementById(id);
  if (e('velocityResult')) e('velocityResult').textContent = Math.round(velocity);
  if (e('frictionResult')) e('frictionResult').textContent = friction.toFixed(3);
  if (e('cfmResult')) e('cfmResult').textContent = Math.round(cfm);
  if (e('maxCfmResult')) e('maxCfmResult').textContent = maxCFMforDuct > 0 ? Math.round(maxCFMforDuct) : '--';
  if (e('suggestedResult')) e('suggestedResult').textContent = sugSize + '"';
  if (e('suggestedUnit')) e('suggestedUnit').textContent = state.shape === 'round' ? 'round' : 'equiv round';
  if (e('maxRunResult')) e('maxRunResult').textContent = maxTEL > 0 ? Math.round(maxTEL) : '--';
  if (e('areaDisplay')) e('areaDisplay').textContent = A.toFixed(2);
  if (e('pressureDropResult')) e('pressureDropResult').textContent = friction.toFixed(3);

  // Velocity card color
  const vc = e('velocityCard');
  if (vc) {
    vc.className = 'result-card';
    if (velocity > maxV) vc.classList.add('danger');
    else if (velocity > maxV * 0.85) vc.classList.add('warning');
    else if (velocity > 0) vc.classList.add('success');
  }

  // Friction card color
  const fc = e('frictionCard');
  if (fc) {
    fc.className = 'result-card';
    if (friction > MAX_FRICTION) fc.classList.add('danger');
    else if (friction > MAX_FRICTION * 0.85) fc.classList.add('warning');
    else if (friction > 0) fc.classList.add('success');
  }

  // Max CFM card color
  const mc = e('maxCfmCard');
  if (mc) {
    mc.className = 'result-card';
    if (maxCFMforDuct > 0 && cfm > maxCFMforDuct) mc.classList.add('danger');
    else if (maxCFMforDuct > 0 && cfm > maxCFMforDuct * 0.85) mc.classList.add('warning');
    else if (maxCFMforDuct > 0) mc.classList.add('success');
  }

  // Status bar
  const sb = e('statusBar');
  const st = e('statusText');
  if (sb && st) {
    let warns = [];
    if (velocity > maxV) warns.push('Velocity ' + Math.round(velocity) + ' FPM > ' + maxV + ' max');
    if (friction > MAX_FRICTION) warns.push('Friction ' + friction.toFixed(3) + ' > 0.08 IWC');
    if (warns.length) { sb.className = 'status-bar error'; st.textContent = '\u26a0 ' + warns.join(' | '); }
    else { sb.className = 'status-bar ok'; st.textContent = 'Within Manual D limits (' + maxV + ' FPM max for ' + state.ductSegment + ')'; }
  }

  drawDial();
}

// ===== UPDATE HEADER RESULTS =====
function drawDial() {
  // Update the compact header pills
  const hv = document.getElementById('hdrVelocity');
  const hf = document.getElementById('hdrFriction');
  const hc = document.getElementById('hdrCFM');
  if (hv) hv.textContent = Math.round(state.velocity);
  if (hf) hf.textContent = state.friction.toFixed(3);
  if (hc) hc.textContent = Math.round(state.cfm);
}


// ===== BRANCH TREE MAP =====
function sysFlexFactor(comp) {
  if (comp===0) return 1;
  if (comp<=15) return 1+(comp/15);
  return 2+(comp-15)/15*2;
}

// ---- Calculation ----
function calcSystem() {
  let totalCFM = 0, longestTEL = 0, critIdx = 0;
  let warns = [];

  SS.runs.forEach((r,ri)=>{
    let straight = 0, fitEL = 0;
    r.steps.forEach(s=>{
      if (s.type==='straight') straight += s.ft;
      else {
        const fit = FITTINGS.find(f=>f.id===s.fid);
        if (fit) fitEL += fit.eq;
      }
    });
    r.totalStraight = straight;
    r.fittingEL = fitEL;
    r.totalTEL = straight + fitEL;

    if (r.totalTEL <= 0) {
      r.frictionRate=0; r.velocity=0; r.cfm=0; r.pressureDrop=0;
      return;
    }

    // System-level return plenum filter PD (applies to ALL return runs)
    var effectiveASP = r.asp;
    if (r.airPath === 'return' && sysRetFilterState.enabled && sysRetFilterState.filterPD > 0) {
      effectiveASP = Math.max(0.01, effectiveASP - sysRetFilterState.filterPD);
    }
    // Per-run filter (individual filter grille on this run)
    if (r.hasFilter) {
      // Pre-estimate filter PD from rated values for initial pass
      var fModels0 = FILTER_DB[r.filterMfg] || [];
      var filt0 = fModels0.find(function(m){ return m.model === r.filterModel; });
      if (filt0 && r.filterPD <= 0) {
        // Use rated PD as first estimate (at rated CFM)
        r.filterPD = filt0.ratedPD;
      }
      if (r.filterPD > 0) {
        effectiveASP = Math.max(0.01, r.asp - r.filterPD);
      }
    }
    var fr = (effectiveASP / r.totalTEL) * 100;

    const D_ft = r.ductSize/12;
    const A = Math.PI*Math.pow(D_ft/2,2);
    const maxV = getMaxVelocity(r.airPath, r.material, ri===0?'trunk':'branch');
    const maxCFMv = maxV * A;

    // Iterate twice to converge filter PD with actual CFM
    var best = 10;
    for (var pass = 0; pass < 2; pass++) {
      var lo=10, hi=maxCFMv;
      best=10;
      for (var it=0;it<50;it++){
        var mid=(lo+hi)/2;
        var fl = frictionLoss(r.ductSize, mid);
        if (r.material==='flex') fl *= sysFlexFactor(r.compression);
        if (fl<=fr){best=mid;lo=mid;}else{hi=mid;}
        if(hi-lo<0.5)break;
      }
      // After first pass, recalc filter PD with actual CFM and re-derive FR
      if (pass === 0 && r.hasFilter && filt0 && best > 10) {
        var ratio0 = best / filt0.ratedCfm;
        r.filterPD = filt0.ratedPD * ratio0 * ratio0;
        effectiveASP = Math.max(0.01, r.asp - r.filterPD);
        fr = (effectiveASP / r.totalTEL) * 100;
      }
    }
    r.frictionRate = fr;

    r.velocity = best/A;
    r.cfm = best;
    var af = frictionLoss(r.ductSize, best);
    if (r.material==='flex') af *= sysFlexFactor(r.compression);
    r.pressureDrop = af * r.totalTEL / 100;

    // Calculate filter face velocity if filter present
    if (r.hasFilter && r.filterGrille && best > 0) {
      var gParts = r.filterGrille.split('x');
      var gArea = (parseInt(gParts[0]) * parseInt(gParts[1])) / 144; // sq ft
      r.filterFaceVel = best / gArea;
      // Final filter PD with converged CFM
      var fModels = FILTER_DB[r.filterMfg] || [];
      var filt = fModels.find(function(m){ return m.model === r.filterModel; });
      if (filt) {
        var ratio = best / filt.ratedCfm;
        r.filterPD = filt.ratedPD * ratio * ratio;
      }
    }

    totalCFM += best;
    if (r.totalTEL > longestTEL) { longestTEL = r.totalTEL; critIdx = ri; }

    if (r.velocity > maxV) warns.push(r.name+': '+Math.round(r.velocity)+' FPM > '+maxV+' max (Manual D)');
    if (r.hasFilter && r.filterFaceVel > 500) warns.push(r.name+': Filter grille '+Math.round(r.filterFaceVel)+' FPM > 500 max');
    if (fr > MAX_FRICTION) warns.push(r.name+': FR '+fr.toFixed(3)+' > 0.08');
  });

  // Update totals
  const e = id => document.getElementById(id);
  if (e('stCFM')) {
    e('stCFM').textContent = Math.round(totalCFM);
    e('stRuns').textContent = SS.runs.length;
    e('stTEL').textContent = longestTEL>0?Math.round(longestTEL):'--';
    const cr = SS.runs[critIdx];
    e('stFR').textContent = cr&&cr.frictionRate>0?cr.frictionRate.toFixed(3):'--';
  }

  // Active run inline results
  if (e('arTEL')) {
    const ar = SS.runs[SS.activeRun];
    e('arTEL').textContent = ar.totalTEL||'--';
    e('arFR').textContent = ar.frictionRate?ar.frictionRate.toFixed(3):'--';
    const velEl = e('arVel'); velEl.textContent = ar.velocity?Math.round(ar.velocity):'--';
    const cfmEl = e('arCFM'); cfmEl.textContent = ar.cfm?Math.round(ar.cfm):'--';

    velEl.className='run-summary-value'; cfmEl.className='run-summary-value';
    e('arFR').className='run-summary-value';
    if (ar.totalTEL>0){
      cfmEl.classList.add('green');
      const mv = getMaxVelocity(ar.airPath, ar.material || 'metal', SS.activeRun===0?'trunk':'branch');
      if(ar.velocity>mv)velEl.classList.add('red');
      else if(ar.velocity>mv*0.85)velEl.classList.add('yellow');
      else velEl.classList.add('green');
      if(ar.frictionRate>MAX_FRICTION)e('arFR').classList.add('red');
      else if(ar.frictionRate>MAX_FRICTION*0.85)e('arFR').classList.add('yellow');
      else e('arFR').classList.add('green');
    }
  }

  // Run summary list
  const list = e('sysRunList');
  if (list) {
    list.innerHTML = SS.runs.map((r,i)=>{
      const isCrit = i===critIdx && r.totalTEL>0;
      const label = r.parentRun!==null?r.branchLabel:r.name;
      return '<div class="sys-run-row" data-goto="'+i+'"><div class="sys-run-row-num">'+(i+1)+'</div><div class="sys-run-row-info"><div class="sys-run-row-name">'+label+' \u2014 '+r.ductSize+'\u2033 '+r.material+' ('+r.airPath+')</div><div class="sys-run-row-stats">TEL:'+Math.round(r.totalTEL)+'ft | FR:'+(r.frictionRate?r.frictionRate.toFixed(3):'--')+' | '+Math.round(r.velocity||0)+'FPM</div></div><div class="sys-run-row-cfm">'+(r.cfm?Math.round(r.cfm)+'CFM':'--')+'</div>'+(isCrit?'<div class="sys-critical-badge">Critical</div>':'')+'</div>';
    }).join('');
  }

  // Manual J
  const tgt = parseFloat((e('mjTarget')||{}).value);
  const mj = e('mjRes');
  if (mj) {
    if (!tgt||tgt<=0){mj.textContent='--';mj.style.color='var(--text-muted)';}
    else {
      const diff=totalCFM-tgt;
      const pct=((diff/tgt)*100).toFixed(1);
      if(diff>=0){mj.textContent='+'+Math.round(diff)+' CFM ('+pct+'%)';mj.style.color='var(--green)';}
      else{mj.textContent=Math.round(diff)+' CFM ('+pct+'%)';mj.style.color='var(--red)';}
    }
  }

  // Status
  const sb = e('sysStatus'), st = e('sysStatusTxt');
  if(sb){
    if(warns.length){sb.className='status-bar error';st.textContent=warns.join(' | ');}
    else if(totalCFM>0){sb.className='status-bar ok';st.textContent='System: ~'+Math.round(totalCFM)+' CFM, '+SS.runs.length+' run'+(SS.runs.length>1?'s':'')+'. Critical: '+(SS.runs[critIdx]?SS.runs[critIdx].name:'--');}
    else{sb.className='status-bar ok';st.textContent='Add steps to analyze';}
  }

  renderRunTabs();
}


function renderBranchTree() {
  var panel = document.getElementById('branchTreePanel');
  var body = document.getElementById('branchTreeBody');
  if (!panel || !body) return;
  if (SS.runs.length < 2) { panel.style.display='none'; return; }
  panel.style.display='';
  
  // Build tree from runs - run 0 is always the trunk
  // Branches reference parentRun
  function buildTree(parentIdx, depth) {
    let h = '';
    const children = SS.runs.filter((r,i)=> i!==parentIdx && r.parentRun===parentIdx);
    children.forEach((child, ci) => {
      const idx = SS.runs.indexOf(child);
      var label = child.branchLabel || ('Branch '+(ci+1));
      h += '<div class="tree-branch-label">'+label+'</div>';
      h += '<div class="tree-node">';
      h += '<div class="tree-item" data-goto="'+idx+'">';
      h += '<div class="tree-item-icon"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M6 3v12M18 9v12M6 9h12"/></svg></div>';
      h += '<div class="tree-item-label">'+child.name+' &mdash; '+child.ductSize+'\u2033 '+(child.material==='flex'?'flex ':'')+child.airPath+'</div>';
      h += '<div class="tree-item-size">'+child.steps.length+' pcs</div>';
      h += '</div>';
      // Recurse for sub-branches
      var subHtml = buildTree(idx, depth+1);
      if (subHtml) h += '<div class="tree-children">'+subHtml+'</div>';
      h += '</div>';
    });
    return h;
  }
  
  // Always show trunk (run 0) first
  const trunk = SS.runs[0];
  let treeHtml = '<div class="tree-trunk">';
  treeHtml += '<div class="tree-item" data-goto="0">';
  treeHtml += '<div class="tree-item-icon"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><rect x="4" y="4" width="16" height="16" rx="2"/></svg></div>';
  treeHtml += '<div class="tree-item-label">'+trunk.name+' (Trunk) &mdash; '+trunk.ductSize+'\u2033 '+trunk.airPath+'</div>';
  treeHtml += '<div class="tree-item-size">'+trunk.steps.length+' pcs</div>';
  treeHtml += '</div></div>';
  
  // Auto-label branches that don't have labels yet
  SS.runs.forEach(function(r,i) {
    if (i > 0 && !r.branchLabel && r.parentRun !== null) {
      r.branchLabel = getNextBranchLabelFor(i);
    }
  });
  
  treeHtml += buildTree(0, 0);
  
  // If no children exist yet, show a hint
  if (SS.runs.length === 1) {
    treeHtml += '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);padding:8px;text-align:center">Add runs to see the branch map</div>';
  }
  
  body.innerHTML = treeHtml;
}

// ---- CFM Estimator ----
function renderCfmEst() {
  const c = document.getElementById('cfmEstRooms');
  if (!c) return;
  const t = HOUSE_TIGHTNESS.find(h=>h.id===cfmEstTightness) || HOUSE_TIGHTNESS[1];
  let totalCFM = 0, totalVol = 0;
  c.innerHTML = cfmRooms.map((rm,i)=>{
    const ht = rm.ceilHt || 8;
    const vol = rm.sqft * ht;
    const cfm = Math.round(vol * t.cACH / 60);
    totalCFM += cfm;
    totalVol += vol;
    return '<div class="cfm-est-room-v2"><button class="cfm-est-remove" data-cfm-rm="'+i+'">\u00d7</button><div class="cfm-est-room-inputs"><input type="text" class="cfm-est-name-input" value="'+rm.name+'" data-cfm-name="'+i+'"><div class="cfm-est-dims"><input type="number" class="cfm-est-sqft-input" value="'+rm.sqft+'" data-cfm-sqft="'+i+'" min="0" max="5000" step="10" placeholder="sqft"><span class="cfm-est-x">\u00d7</span><input type="number" class="cfm-est-ht-input" value="'+ht+'" data-cfm-ht="'+i+'" min="6" max="20" step="0.5" placeholder="ht"><span class="cfm-est-unit">ft</span></div><div class="cfm-est-vol">'+vol+' ft\u00b3</div></div><div class="cfm-est-cfm">'+cfm+'<span class="cfm-est-cfm-unit">CFM</span></div></div>';
  }).join('');
  const tot = document.getElementById('cfmEstTot');
  if (tot) tot.textContent = totalCFM + ' CFM (\u2248' + Math.round(totalVol) + ' ft\u00b3 total volume)';
  // Render tightness selector
  const ts = document.getElementById('tightnessSelect');
  if (ts) {
    ts.innerHTML = HOUSE_TIGHTNESS.map(h=>
      '<button class="tightness-btn'+(h.id===cfmEstTightness?' active':'')+'" data-tightness="'+h.id+'"><div class="tightness-btn-label">'+h.label+'</div><div class="tightness-btn-ach">H:'+h.hACH+' / C:'+h.cACH+'</div></button>'
    ).join('');
  }
  const td = document.getElementById('tightnessDesc');
  if (td) td.textContent = t.desc;
  const tach = document.getElementById('tightnessACH');
  if (tach) tach.innerHTML = 'Heating: <strong>'+t.hACH+' ACH</strong> | Cooling: <strong>'+t.cACH+' ACH</strong>';
}

// System state
let SS = {
  collars: [],
  retCollars: [],
  runs: [],
  activeRun: 0,
  addMode: null, // null, 'straight', 'fitting'
  searchTerm: '',
};

// CFM estimator rooms
let cfmRooms = [
  {name:'Living Room',sqft:300,ceilHt:8},{name:'Master Bed',sqft:200,ceilHt:8},{name:'Bedroom 2',sqft:150,ceilHt:8},
];

// Manual J Table 5A - Default ACH rates
const HOUSE_TIGHTNESS = [
  {id:'tight',label:'Tight',hACH:0.15,cACH:0.08,desc:'All seams/joints/penetrations sealed, tight backdraft dampers, direct-vent gas, sealed fireplace'},
  {id:'semi-tight',label:'Semi-Tight',hACH:0.30,cACH:0.16,desc:'Good air sealing, typical new construction to energy code (3-5 ACH50)'},
  {id:'average',label:'Average',hACH:0.45,cACH:0.25,desc:'Standard construction, some sealing of major penetrations (5-9 ACH50)'},
  {id:'semi-loose',label:'Semi-Loose',hACH:0.70,cACH:0.37,desc:'Older home, minimal air sealing, some drafts noticeable'},
  {id:'loose',label:'Loose',hACH:0.95,cACH:0.50,desc:'Older home, no air sealing, obvious drafts, unsealed penetrations (>12 ACH50)'},
];
let cfmEstTightness = 'semi-tight';


function mkRun(idx, parentIdx, branchLabel) {
  return {
    name: 'Run '+(idx+1),
    airPath: 'supply', material: 'metal', compression: 4,
    ductSize: 8, asp: 0.50,
    steps: [],
    parentRun: parentIdx !== undefined ? parentIdx : null,
    branchLabel: branchLabel || '',
    collapsed: false,
    // Filter at end of run (for returns with filter grille)
    hasFilter: false,
    filterMfg: 'generic',
    filterModel: '4in-M11',
    filterGrille: '20x25',
    filterPD: 0,
    filterFaceVel: 0,
    // calc
    totalStraight:0, fittingEL:0, totalTEL:0,
    frictionRate:0, velocity:0, cfm:0, pressureDrop:0,
  };
}

function getNextBranchLabel(parentIdx) {
  // Count existing direct children of parentIdx
  var parentRun = SS.runs[parentIdx];
  var existingChildren = SS.runs.filter(function(r) { return r.parentRun === parentIdx; });
  var childNum = existingChildren.length + 1;
  if (parentIdx === 0 || !parentRun.branchLabel) {
    // Direct child of trunk: "Branch 1", "Branch 2"
    return 'Branch ' + childNum;
  } else {
    // Sub-branch: parse parent label to get numbering
    var parentLabel = parentRun.branchLabel;
    var parentNum = parentLabel.replace('Branch ', '');
    return 'Branch ' + parentNum + '-' + childNum;
  }
}


function rebuildParentIndices() {
  // After removing runs, parentRun indices may be wrong
  // We need to re-assign based on saved reference
  // Strategy: each run stores parentRun as index, but after splice those shift
  // So we tag each run with a unique id before remove, and remap after
  // Since this is called AFTER splice, we rebuild labels instead
  var trunkIdx = 0;
  SS.runs.forEach(function(r, ri) {
    if (r.parentRun !== null) {
      // Check parent still exists and is valid
      if (r.parentRun >= SS.runs.length) r.parentRun = 0;
    }
  });
  relabelBranches();
}

function relabelBranches() {
  SS.runs.forEach(function(r, ri) {
    if (r.parentRun !== null) {
      r.branchLabel = getNextBranchLabelFor(ri);
    }
  });
}

function getNextBranchLabelFor(runIdx) {
  var r = SS.runs[runIdx];
  if (r.parentRun === null) return '';
  var parentRun = SS.runs[r.parentRun];
  // Count siblings before this one
  var siblingsBefore = 0;
  for (var si = 0; si < runIdx; si++) {
    if (SS.runs[si].parentRun === r.parentRun) siblingsBefore++;
  }
  var childNum = siblingsBefore + 1;
  if (r.parentRun === 0 || !parentRun.branchLabel) {
    return 'Branch ' + childNum;
  } else {
    var parentNum = parentRun.branchLabel.replace('Branch ', '');
    return 'Branch ' + parentNum + '-' + childNum;
  }
}

function addBranch(parentIdx) {
  saveRunFromDOM();
  var label = getNextBranchLabel(parentIdx);
  var nr = mkRun(SS.runs.length, parentIdx, label);
  // Inherit air path and material from parent
  var parent = SS.runs[parentIdx];
  nr.airPath = parent.airPath;
  nr.material = parent.material;
  nr.asp = parent.asp;
  nr.ductSize = Math.max(parent.ductSize - 2, 4); // default smaller
  SS.runs.push(nr);
  SS.activeRun = SS.runs.length - 1;
  SS.addMode = null;
  SS.searchTerm = '';
  renderSystem();
}

function initSystem() {
  SS.runs = [mkRun(0)];
  SS.activeRun = 0;
  SS.collars = [];
  SS.retCollars = [];
  renderSystem();
}

// ---- Render ----
function renderSystem() {
  renderRunTabs();
  renderRunArea();
  calcSystem();
  updateSysFilterDisclaimer();
  // renderCfmEst moved to Rooms tab
}

function renderCollars() {
  const el = document.getElementById('collarChips');
  document.getElementById('collarCt').textContent = SS.collars.length;
  if (!SS.collars.length) { el.innerHTML='<span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-dim)">No collars</span>'; return; }
  const typeLabels = {'sq-to-round':'Sq\u2192Rnd','tab':'Tab','finger-saver':'Finger','spin-in':'Spin'};
  el.innerHTML = SS.collars.map((c,i)=>{
    const lbl = typeLabels[c.type] || c.type;
    return '<div class="collar-chip">'+c.size+'\u2033 '+lbl+'<button class="collar-chip-x" data-col-rm="'+i+'">\u00d7</button></div>';
  }).join('');
}

function renderRetCollars() {
  const el = document.getElementById('retCollarChips');
  if (!el) return;
  var ct = document.getElementById('retCollarCt');
  if (ct) ct.textContent = SS.retCollars.length;
  if (!SS.retCollars.length) { el.innerHTML='<span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-dim)">No collars</span>'; return; }
  const typeLabels = {'sq-to-round':'Sq\u2192Rnd','tab':'Tab','finger-saver':'Finger','spin-in':'Spin'};
  el.innerHTML = SS.retCollars.map((c,i)=>{
    const lbl = typeLabels[c.type] || c.type;
    return '<div class="collar-chip">'+c.size+'\u2033 '+lbl+'<button class="collar-chip-x" data-ret-col-rm="'+i+'">\u00d7</button></div>';
  }).join('');
}

function renderRunTabs() {
  var c = document.getElementById('sysRunTabs');
  if (!c) return;
  var h = '';
  // Build hierarchical tab display
  function renderRunTab(ri) {
    var r = SS.runs[ri];
    var active = ri===SS.activeRun?' active':'';
    var hasData = r.steps.length>0?' has-data':'';
    var isBranch = r.parentRun!==null?' branch-tab':'';
    var label = r.parentRun!==null ? (r.branchLabel || r.name) : r.name;
    var collapsed = r.collapsed && ri!==SS.activeRun;
    h += '<button class="sys-run-tab'+active+hasData+isBranch+'" data-rt="'+ri+'">'+label+'</button>';
    // Render children indented
    var children = [];
    SS.runs.forEach(function(cr, ci) { if (cr.parentRun === ri) children.push(ci); });
    if (children.length > 0) {
      h += '<div class="branch-indent">';
      children.forEach(function(ci) { renderRunTab(ci); });
      h += '</div>';
    }
  }
  // Start with trunk runs (parentRun === null)
  SS.runs.forEach(function(r,i) {
    if (r.parentRun === null) {
      renderRunTab(i);
    }
  });
  if (SS.runs.length < 20) h += '<button class="sys-add-btn" id="sysAddRun">+ Trunk</button>';
  c.innerHTML = h;
}

function renderRunArea() {
  const r = SS.runs[SS.activeRun];
  if (!r) return;
  const c = document.getElementById('sysRunArea');
  if (!c) return;
  const i = SS.activeRun;
  const canRemove = SS.runs.length > 1;

  // Duct sizes
  const sizes = [4,5,6,7,8,9,10,12,14,16,18,20,22,24];
  const sizeOpts = sizes.map(s=>'<option value="'+s+'"'+(r.ductSize===s?' selected':'')+'>'+s+'\"</option>').join('');

  // Compression
  const compHTML = r.material==='flex' ? '<div style="margin-top:6px"><div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:4px"><span class="input-label">Flex Compression</span><span style="font-family:\'JetBrains Mono\',monospace;font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:var(--orange)">'+r.compression+'%</span></div><div style="display:flex;gap:4px;flex-wrap:wrap">'+[4,5,10,15,20,25,30].map(p=>'<button class="compression-preset-btn'+(r.compression===p?' active':'')+'" data-sc="'+p+'">'+p+'%</button>').join('')+'</div></div>' : '';

  // Branch context info
  var branchCtx = '';
  if (r.parentRun !== null) {
    var parentR = SS.runs[r.parentRun];
    var parentLabel = parentR ? (parentR.branchLabel || parentR.name) : 'Trunk';
    branchCtx = '<div class="branch-ctx-bar"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" style="width:14px;height:14px;flex-shrink:0"><path d="M6 3v12M18 9v12M6 9h12"/></svg><span>Branch of <strong>'+parentLabel+'</strong> ('+parentR.ductSize+'\u2033 '+parentR.airPath+')</span></div>';
  }

  // Children branches
  var childBranches = [];
  SS.runs.forEach(function(cr, ci) { if (cr.parentRun === i) childBranches.push(ci); });
  var childHTML = '';
  if (childBranches.length > 0) {
    childHTML = '<div class="branch-children-section"><div class="input-label" style="margin-bottom:6px">Branches from this run</div>';
    childBranches.forEach(function(ci) {
      var cr = SS.runs[ci];
      childHTML += '<div class="branch-child-card" data-rt="'+ci+'"><div class="branch-child-label">'+cr.branchLabel+'</div><div class="branch-child-info">'+cr.ductSize+'\u2033 '+cr.material+' '+cr.airPath+' \u2014 '+cr.steps.length+' steps</div></div>';
    });
    childHTML += '</div>';
  }

  // Steps path
  let pathHTML = '';
  r.steps.forEach((s,si)=>{
    const isLast = si === r.steps.length - 1;
    let dotClass = s.type==='straight'?'straight':'fitting';
    if (s.fid && FITTINGS.find(f=>f.id===s.fid && f.branch)) dotClass = 'branch';
    if (s.fid && (s.fid.startsWith('sr')||s.fid.startsWith('d')||s.fid.startsWith('rg')||s.fid.startsWith('fg')||s.fid.startsWith('b'))) dotClass = 'terminal';

    let name, detail, eq, noteHTML='';
    if (s.type==='straight') {
      name = 'Straight Duct';
      detail = s.ft+' ft';
      eq = s.ft+' ft';
    } else {
      const fit = FITTINGS.find(f=>f.id===s.fid);
      name = fit ? fit.name : 'Fitting';
      detail = (fit?fit.eq:0)+' ft EQ';
      eq = (fit?fit.eq:0)+' ft';
      if (fit && fit.note) noteHTML = '<div class="path-step-note">'+fit.note+'</div>';
    }

    pathHTML += '<div class="path-step"><div class="path-step-line"><div class="path-step-dot '+dotClass+'"></div>'+(isLast?'':'<div class="path-step-connector"></div>')+'</div><div class="path-step-body"><div class="path-step-info"><div class="path-step-name">'+name+'</div><div class="path-step-detail">'+detail+'</div>'+noteHTML+'</div><div class="path-step-eq">'+eq+'</div><button class="path-step-remove" data-step-rm="'+si+'">\u00d7</button></div></div>';
  });

  if (r.steps.length === 0) {
    pathHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:16px;color:var(--text-dim);font-size:12px">No steps yet. Start building this run below.</div>';
  }

  // Per-run results
  var filterResHTML = '';
  if (r.hasFilter && r.cfm > 0) {
    var fvClass = r.filterFaceVel > 500 ? 'danger' : (r.filterFaceVel > 400 ? 'warn' : 'ok');
    filterResHTML = '<div class="filter-impact-card"><div class="filter-impact-title">\u2692 Filter Impact</div>'+
      '<div class="filter-impact-row"><span class="filter-impact-label">Filter PD</span><span class="filter-impact-value" style="color:'+(r.filterPD>0.25?'var(--red-glow)':'var(--text)')+'">'+(r.filterPD?r.filterPD.toFixed(2):'--')+' IWC</span></div>'+
      '<div class="filter-impact-row"><span class="filter-impact-label">Face Velocity</span><span class="filter-impact-value '+fvClass+'">'+(r.filterFaceVel?Math.round(r.filterFaceVel):'--')+' FPM</span></div>'+
      '<div class="filter-impact-row"><span class="filter-impact-label">Effective ASP</span><span class="filter-impact-value">'+(r.filterPD?(r.asp - r.filterPD).toFixed(2):'--')+' IWC</span></div>'+
      '<div class="filter-impact-row"><span class="filter-impact-label">ASP w/o Filter</span><span class="filter-impact-value" style="color:var(--text-muted)">'+r.asp.toFixed(2)+' IWC</span></div>'+
      (r.filterFaceVel > 500 ? '<div class="filter-warning-banner danger" style="margin-top:8px"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" width="14" height="14"><path d="M10.29 3.86L1.82 18a2 2 0 001.71 3h16.94a2 2 0 001.71-3L13.71 3.86a2 2 0 00-3.42 0z"/><line x1="12" y1="9" x2="12" y2="13"/><line x1="12" y1="17" x2="12.01" y2="17"/></svg><span>Filter face velocity exceeds 500 FPM. Increase grille size or reduce CFM. ASHRAE 52.2 tests filters at 300-492 FPM.</span></div>' : '')+
      '</div>';
  }
  const resHTML = '<div class="run-summary-grid" style="margin-top:10px"><div class="run-summary-card"><div class="run-summary-value" id="arTEL">'+(r.totalTEL||'--')+'</div><div class="run-summary-unit">ft</div><div class="run-summary-label">Total EQ Length</div></div><div class="run-summary-card"><div class="run-summary-value" id="arFR">'+(r.frictionRate?r.frictionRate.toFixed(3):'--')+'</div><div class="run-summary-unit">IWC/100ft</div><div class="run-summary-label">Friction Rate</div></div><div class="run-summary-card"><div class="run-summary-value" id="arVel">'+(r.velocity?Math.round(r.velocity):'--')+'</div><div class="run-summary-unit">FPM</div><div class="run-summary-label">Velocity</div></div><div class="run-summary-card"><div class="run-summary-value green" id="arCFM">'+(r.cfm?Math.round(r.cfm):'--')+'</div><div class="run-summary-unit">CFM</div><div class="run-summary-label">CFM Capacity</div></div></div>'+filterResHTML;

  c.innerHTML = '<div class="sys-run-header-bar"><div class="sys-run-title">'+(r.parentRun!==null?r.branchLabel:r.name)+'</div><div style="display:flex;gap:6px">'+(canRemove?'<button class="sys-remove-btn" data-rm-run="'+i+'">Remove</button>':'')+'<button class="sys-branch-btn" data-add-branch="'+i+'">+ Branch</button></div></div>'+
    branchCtx+
    '<div class="sys-config-grid"><div class="input-group"><label class="input-label">Air Path</label><div class="seg-control" id="sysAP"><button class="seg-btn'+(r.airPath==='supply'?' active':'')+'" data-sap="supply">Supply</button><button class="seg-btn'+(r.airPath==='return'?' active':'')+'" data-sap="return">Return</button></div></div><div class="input-group"><label class="input-label">Material</label><div class="seg-control" id="sysMat"><button class="seg-btn'+(r.material==='metal'?' active':'')+'" data-smat="metal">Metal</button><button class="seg-btn'+(r.material==='flex'?' active':'')+'" data-smat="flex">Flex</button></div></div><div class="input-group"><label class="input-label">Duct Size</label><select class="input-field" id="sysDSize">'+sizeOpts+'</select></div><div class="input-group"><label class="input-label">Avail Static (IWC)</label><input type="number" class="input-field" id="sysASP" value="'+r.asp+'" min="0.05" max="2.00" step="0.05"></div></div>'+
    compHTML+
    buildSysFilterHTML(r, i)+
    '<div style="margin-top:12px"><div class="input-label" style="margin-bottom:6px">Duct Path (step-by-step)</div>'+pathHTML+'</div>'+
    '<div class="add-step-area"><div class="add-step-header">\u2795 Add to Run</div>'+
    '<div class="quick-add-section"><div class="quick-add-label">Quick Add</div><div class="quick-add-grid"><button class="quick-add-btn" data-qa-straight="1"><div class="quick-add-icon"><svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="1.5"><line x1="4" y1="16" x2="28" y2="16"/><path d="M24 12 L28 16 L24 20" stroke-width="1"/></svg></div>Straight</button><button class="quick-add-btn" data-qa-fit="e1"><div class="quick-add-icon"><svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round"><path d="M8 6 L8 16 Q8 24 16 24 L26 24"/></svg></div>90\u00b0 Elbow</button><button class="quick-add-btn" data-qa-fit="e7"><div class="quick-add-icon"><svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round"><path d="M6 8 L6 18 Q6 24 12 24 L26 24"/></svg></div>45\u00b0 Elbow</button><button class="quick-add-btn" data-qa-fit="w1"><div class="quick-add-icon"><svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round"><path d="M8 6 L8 26"/><path d="M8 16 L24 26"/><circle cx="8" cy="16" r="2" fill="currentColor" stroke="none"/></svg></div>Wye</button><button class="quick-add-btn" data-qa-fit="rd1"><div class="quick-add-icon"><svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="1.5"><path d="M6 8 L6 24 L26 20 L26 12 Z"/></svg></div>Reducer</button><button class="quick-add-btn" data-qa-fit="b2"><div class="quick-add-icon"><svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="1.5"><path d="M14 6 L14 16 L6 16 L6 26 L26 26 L26 16 L18 16 L18 6 Z"/></svg></div>90\u00b0 Boot</button></div></div>'+
    '<div class="add-divider-line"></div>'+
    '<div class="add-step-type-row"><button class="add-step-type-btn'+(SS.addMode==='straight'?' active':'')+'" data-asm="straight">\u2795 Straight Duct</button><button class="add-step-type-btn'+(SS.addMode==='fitting'?' active':'')+'" data-asm="fitting">\u2795 All Fittings</button></div>'+
    (SS.addMode==='straight'?'<div class="straight-input-row"><span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted)">Length:</span><input type="number" id="straightFtIn" value="10" min="1" max="500" step="1"><span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted)">ft</span><button class="add-fitting-btn" id="addStraightBtn" style="padding:8px 12px">Add</button></div>':'')+
    (SS.addMode==='fitting'?'<input type="text" class="fitting-search-input" id="fitSearch" placeholder="Type to search fittings..." value="'+SS.searchTerm+'"><div class="fitting-results" id="fitResults">'+renderFittingResults()+'</div>':'')+
    '</div>'+resHTML+childHTML;
}


// SVG icons for fittings (compact inline diagrams)
function fittingSvg(f) {
  const s = 'stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round"';
  const cat = f.cat;
  const id = f.id;
  // Elbows
  if (cat === 'Elbows') {
    if (id.includes('e7') || id.includes('e9') || f.name.includes('45')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M6 8 L6 18 Q6 24 12 24 L26 24"/><path d="M24 21 L26 24 L24 27" stroke-width="1"/></svg>';
    }
    if (f.name.includes('Mitered') && f.name.includes('vanes')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M8 6 L8 16 L24 16"/><line x1="10" y1="14" x2="12" y2="16"/><line x1="13" y1="13" x2="15" y2="15"/><line x1="16" y1="12" x2="18" y2="14"/><path d="M22 13 L24 16 L22 19" stroke-width="1"/></svg>';
    }
    if (f.name.includes('Mitered')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M8 6 L8 16 L24 16"/><path d="M22 13 L24 16 L22 19" stroke-width="1"/></svg>';
    }
    if (f.name.includes('Flex')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M8 6 C8 16 8 20 14 22 C20 24 24 24 26 24" stroke-dasharray="2 1"/><path d="M24 21 L26 24 L24 27" stroke-width="1"/></svg>';
    }
    if (f.name.includes('Rect')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M6 6 L6 10 L6 18 Q6 24 12 24 L26 24"/><path d="M4 6 L8 6 M4 18 L8 18"/><path d="M12 22 L12 26 M24 22 L24 26"/></svg>';
    }
    // Default 90 round elbow
    return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M8 6 L8 16 Q8 24 16 24 L26 24"/><path d="M24 21 L26 24 L24 27" stroke-width="1"/></svg>';
  }
  // Wyes & Tees
  if (cat === 'Wyes & Tees') {
    if (f.name.includes('Bullhead')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M16 6 L16 16"/><path d="M4 26 L16 16 L28 26"/><circle cx="16" cy="16" r="2" fill="currentColor" stroke="none"/></svg>';
    }
    if (f.name.includes('45') || f.name.includes('Wye')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M8 6 L8 26"/><path d="M8 16 L24 26"/><circle cx="8" cy="16" r="2" fill="currentColor" stroke="none"/></svg>';
    }
    if (f.name.includes('straight through')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M8 6 L8 26"/><path d="M8 16 L24 16"/><circle cx="8" cy="16" r="2" fill="currentColor" stroke="none"/></svg>';
    }
    // Default tee
    return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M8 6 L8 26"/><path d="M8 16 L24 16"/><circle cx="8" cy="16" r="2" fill="currentColor" stroke="none"/></svg>';
  }
  // Takeoffs & Collars
  if (cat === 'Takeoffs & Collars') {
    if (f.name.includes('45')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><rect x="6" y="4" width="20" height="10" rx="2"/><path d="M16 14 L20 28"/></svg>';
    }
    return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><rect x="6" y="4" width="20" height="10" rx="2"/><path d="M16 14 L16 28"/></svg>';
  }
  // Boots - each type gets a unique icon
  if (cat === 'Boots') {
    if (f.name.includes('90') && f.name.includes('Extended')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M14 4 L14 14 L4 14 L4 24 L28 24 L28 14 L18 14 L18 4"/><line x1="4" y1="14" x2="4" y2="8" stroke-dasharray="2 1.5"/><line x1="28" y1="14" x2="28" y2="8" stroke-dasharray="2 1.5"/></svg>';
    }
    if (f.name.includes('90') && f.name.includes('round')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><ellipse cx="16" cy="8" rx="4" ry="3"/><path d="M12 8 L12 16 L6 16 L6 26 L26 26 L26 16 L20 16 L20 8"/></svg>';
    }
    if (f.name.includes('Straight') || (f.name.includes('straight') && !f.name.includes('90'))) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><ellipse cx="16" cy="8" rx="4" ry="3"/><path d="M12 8 L8 26 L24 26 L20 8"/></svg>';
    }
    if (f.name.includes('Side') || f.name.includes('Takeoff')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M6 10 L6 22 L16 22 L16 10 Z"/><path d="M16 14 L28 14 L28 18 L16 18"/><path d="M25 12 L28 16 L25 20" stroke-width="1"/></svg>';
    }
    if (f.name.includes('Pan') || f.name.includes('Stack')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M14 4 L14 12 L18 12 L18 4"/><rect x="6" y="12" width="20" height="6" rx="1"/><rect x="4" y="18" width="24" height="8" rx="1"/><line x1="8" y1="22" x2="24" y2="22" stroke-dasharray="2 2" stroke-width="1"/></svg>';
    }
    if (f.name.includes('Ceiling') || f.name.includes('top entry')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><rect x="6" y="12" width="20" height="14" rx="2"/><path d="M14 4 L14 12 M18 4 L18 12"/><line x1="6" y1="26" x2="26" y2="26" stroke-width="2"/></svg>';
    }
    return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M14 4 L14 16 L6 26 L26 26 L18 16 L18 4"/></svg>';
  }
  // Supply Registers
  if (cat === 'Supply Registers') {
    if (f.name.includes('Wall')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><rect x="4" y="8" width="24" height="16" rx="2"/><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="8" y2="20"/><line x1="12" y1="12" x2="12" y2="20"/><line x1="16" y1="12" x2="16" y2="20"/><line x1="20" y1="12" x2="20" y2="20"/><line x1="24" y1="12" x2="24" y2="20"/></svg>';
    }
    return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><rect x="4" y="8" width="24" height="16" rx="2"/><line x1="8" y1="8" x2="8" y2="24"/><line x1="12" y1="8" x2="12" y2="24"/><line x1="16" y1="8" x2="16" y2="24"/><line x1="20" y1="8" x2="20" y2="24"/><line x1="24" y1="8" x2="24" y2="24"/></svg>';
  }
  // Ceiling Diffusers
  if (cat === 'Ceiling Diffusers') {
    if (f.name.includes('Round')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><circle cx="16" cy="16" r="10"/><circle cx="16" cy="16" r="6"/><circle cx="16" cy="16" r="2"/></svg>';
    }
    if (f.name.includes('Linear') || f.name.includes('Slot')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><rect x="2" y="10" width="28" height="12" rx="2"/><line x1="6" y1="14" x2="6" y2="22"/><line x1="10" y1="14" x2="10" y2="22"/><line x1="14" y1="14" x2="14" y2="22"/><line x1="18" y1="14" x2="18" y2="22"/><line x1="22" y1="14" x2="22" y2="22"/><line x1="26" y1="14" x2="26" y2="22"/></svg>';
    }
    return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><rect x="4" y="4" width="24" height="24" rx="2"/><rect x="8" y="8" width="16" height="16" rx="1"/><rect x="12" y="12" width="8" height="8" rx="1"/></svg>';
  }
  // Return Grilles
  if (cat === 'Return Grilles') {
    return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><rect x="4" y="4" width="24" height="24" rx="2"/><line x1="4" y1="10" x2="28" y2="10"/><line x1="4" y1="16" x2="28" y2="16"/><line x1="4" y1="22" x2="28" y2="22"/></svg>';
  }
  // Filter Grilles
  if (cat === 'Filter Grilles') {
    return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><rect x="4" y="4" width="24" height="24" rx="2"/><line x1="4" y1="10" x2="28" y2="10"/><line x1="4" y1="16" x2="28" y2="16"/><line x1="4" y1="22" x2="28" y2="22"/><line x1="10" y1="4" x2="10" y2="28" stroke-dasharray="2 2"/><line x1="22" y1="4" x2="22" y2="28" stroke-dasharray="2 2"/></svg>';
  }
  // Return Fittings
  if (cat === 'Return Fittings') {
    if (f.name.includes('Panning') || f.name.includes('Joist')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M4 10 L4 22 L28 22 L28 10"/><line x1="4" y1="6" x2="28" y2="6"/><line x1="4" y1="6" x2="4" y2="10"/><line x1="28" y1="6" x2="28" y2="10"/></svg>';
    }
    return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M12 6 L12 16 L20 16 L20 6"/><path d="M6 16 L26 16 L26 26 L6 26 Z"/></svg>';
  }
  // Reducers
  if (cat === 'Reducers') {
    if (f.name.includes('Abrupt')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M6 8 L6 24 L16 24 L16 20 L26 20 L26 12 L16 12 L16 8 Z"/></svg>';
    }
    return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><path d="M6 8 L6 24 L26 20 L26 12 Z"/></svg>';
  }
  // Dampers
  if (cat === 'Dampers') {
    if (f.name.includes('Backdraft')) {
      return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><circle cx="16" cy="16" r="10"/><path d="M10 16 L22 12" stroke-width="2"/></svg>';
    }
    return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><circle cx="16" cy="16" r="10"/><line x1="10" y1="16" x2="22" y2="16" stroke-width="2"/></svg>';
  }
  return '<svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" '+s+'><circle cx="16" cy="16" r="8"/></svg>';
}


// ===== FITTING DETAIL INFO =====
function getFittingDetail(f) {
  var details = {
    'b1': 'Straight boot: Round duct connects straight down into rectangular register. Gradual taper. Used for floor registers directly below duct runs. Lowest restriction of all boots.',
    'b2': '90\u00b0 boot: Round duct makes a 90\u00b0 turn to rectangular register. Common but high restriction \u2014 the turn causes turbulence. Use when duct runs horizontally to floor/wall register.',
    'b3': '90\u00b0 w/ Extended Plenum: Same 90\u00b0 turn but with extended plenum connections on both sides. Slightly lower restriction than standard 90\u00b0. Common on trunk-and-branch systems.',
    'b4': 'Side Takeoff boot: Branches off the side of a trunk line to a register. Air exits perpendicular. Good for wall registers along a trunk line.',
    'b5': 'Ceiling diffuser box: Top-entry box connects round duct from above to a ceiling diffuser. Air drops down and spreads outward. For ceiling-mounted supply.',
    'b6': 'Stack boot / pan: Rectangular transition to a wall stack (thin duct inside wall cavities). Used for wall registers on upper floors.',
    'e1': 'R/D=1.5 (smooth): Centerline radius is 1.5x the diameter. Best practice \u2014 lowest turbulence and pressure drop of all 90\u00b0 turns.',
    'e2': '5-piece gored: Made from 5 stamped pieces. Nearly as good as smooth. Seams create slightly more turbulence.',
    'e3': '3-piece: Made from 3 pieces. More abrupt turn. Moderate restriction. Common in residential.',
    'e4': 'R/D=1.0 (short): Centerline radius equals the diameter. Tighter turn = more restriction. Used in tight spaces. 2x EQ length of R/D=1.5.',
    'e5': 'Mitered, no vanes: Sharp 90\u00b0 square turn with no turning vanes. Very high restriction. Avoid when possible.',
    'e6': 'Mitered, w/ vanes: Square 90\u00b0 turn with internal turning vanes. Much lower restriction than without vanes.',
  };
  return details[f.id] || null;
}

function renderFittingResults() {
  const term = SS.searchTerm.toLowerCase();
  let lastCat = '';
  let html = '';
  let count = 0;
  FITTINGS.forEach(f => {
    if (term && !f.name.toLowerCase().includes(term) && !f.cat.toLowerCase().includes(term) && !(f.note||'').toLowerCase().includes(term)) return;
    if (f.cat !== lastCat) {
      html += '<div class="fitting-cat-header">'+f.cat+'</div>';
      lastCat = f.cat;
    }
    var detail = getFittingDetail(f);
    html += '<div class="fitting-result-card" data-add-fit="'+f.id+'"><div class="fitting-icon">'+fittingSvg(f)+'</div><div class="fitting-result-info"><div class="fitting-result-name">'+f.name+'</div>'+(f.note?'<div class="fitting-result-note">'+f.note+'</div>':'')+(detail?'<div class="fitting-detail-expand" id="fd-'+f.id+'" style="display:none;padding:6px;margin-top:4px;background:var(--bg);border-radius:4px;border:1px solid var(--border);font-size:10px;color:var(--text-muted);line-height:1.4">'+detail+'</div>':'')+'</div><div class="fitting-result-eq" style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:flex-end;gap:2px"><span>'+f.eq+' ft</span>'+(detail?'<span class="fitting-info-btn" data-fit-info="'+f.id+'" style="width:16px;height:16px;border-radius:50%;background:rgba(255,255,255,0.05);border:1px solid var(--border);color:var(--text-dim);font-size:9px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;cursor:pointer">i</span>':'')+'</div></div>';
    count++;
  });
  if (count === 0) html = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:16px;color:var(--text-dim);font-size:12px">No matches found</div>';
  return html;
}

// ---- Event Delegation ----
document.getElementById('page-system').addEventListener('click', function(ev) {
  if (wizHandleClick(ev)) return;
  const t = ev.target;
  // Run tabs
  const rt = t.closest('[data-rt]');
  if (rt) { saveRunFromDOM(); SS.activeRun=parseInt(rt.dataset.rt); SS.addMode=null; SS.searchTerm=''; renderRunArea(); calcSystem(); return; }
  // Add run
  if (t.closest('#sysAddRun')) { saveRunFromDOM(); var nr=mkRun(SS.runs.length, null, ''); SS.runs.push(nr); SS.activeRun=SS.runs.length-1; SS.addMode=null; SS.searchTerm=''; renderSystem(); return; }
  // Add branch from a run
  var ab = t.closest('[data-add-branch]');
  if (ab) { addBranch(parseInt(ab.dataset.addBranch)); return; }
  // Remove run
  var rmr = t.closest('[data-rm-run]');
  if (rmr) {
    var idx=parseInt(rmr.dataset.rmRun);
    // Also remove all children (branches) of this run recursively
    function getDescendants(parentIdx) {
      var desc = [];
      SS.runs.forEach(function(r,ri) {
        if (r.parentRun === parentIdx) { desc.push(ri); desc = desc.concat(getDescendants(ri)); }
      });
      return desc;
    }
    var toRemove = [idx].concat(getDescendants(idx));
    toRemove.sort(function(a,b){return b-a;}); // remove from end first
    toRemove.forEach(function(ri) { SS.runs.splice(ri,1); });
    // Fix parentRun references after splice
    SS.runs.forEach(function(r,ri) {
      r.name = 'Run '+(ri+1);
      if (r.parentRun !== null) {
        // Find new index of parent
        // parentRun was an index that may have shifted
        // We need to handle this - safest: rebuild labels
      }
    });
    // Rebuild parentRun indices after splice
    rebuildParentIndices();
    if(SS.activeRun>=SS.runs.length)SS.activeRun=SS.runs.length-1;
    SS.addMode=null; renderSystem(); return;
  }
  // Air path
  const ap = t.closest('[data-sap]');
  if (ap) { SS.runs[SS.activeRun].airPath=ap.dataset.sap; renderRunArea(); calcSystem(); updateSysFilterDisclaimer(); return; }
  // Material
  const mat = t.closest('[data-smat]');
  if (mat) { const r=SS.runs[SS.activeRun]; r.material=mat.dataset.smat; if(r.material==='metal')r.compression=0; else if(r.material==='flex'&&r.compression<4)r.compression=4; renderRunArea(); calcSystem(); return; }
  // Compression
  const sc = t.closest('[data-sc]');
  if (sc) { SS.runs[SS.activeRun].compression=parseInt(sc.dataset.sc); renderRunArea(); calcSystem(); return; }
  // Remove step
  const srm = t.closest('[data-step-rm]');
  if (srm) { SS.runs[SS.activeRun].steps.splice(parseInt(srm.dataset.stepRm),1); renderRunArea(); calcSystem(); return; }
  // Add mode toggle
  const asm = t.closest('[data-asm]');
  if (asm) { SS.addMode = SS.addMode===asm.dataset.asm ? null : asm.dataset.asm; SS.searchTerm=''; renderRunArea(); if(SS.addMode==='fitting'){setTimeout(()=>{const si=document.getElementById('fitSearch');if(si)si.focus();},100);} return; }
  // Add straight
  if (t.closest('#addStraightBtn')) { const inp=document.getElementById('straightFtIn'); const ft=parseFloat(inp?inp.value:0)||0; if(ft>0){SS.runs[SS.activeRun].steps.push({type:'straight',ft:ft}); renderRunArea(); calcSystem();} return; }
  // Quick-add straight
  const qas = t.closest('[data-qa-straight]');
  if (qas) { SS.addMode='straight'; renderRunArea(); setTimeout(()=>{const inp=document.getElementById('straightFtIn');if(inp)inp.focus();},100); return; }
  // Quick-add fitting
  const qaf = t.closest('[data-qa-fit]');
  if (qaf) { const fid=qaf.dataset.qaFit; const fit=FITTINGS.find(f=>f.id===fid); if(fit){SS.runs[SS.activeRun].steps.push({type:'fitting',fid:fid}); renderRunArea(); calcSystem();} return; }
  // Add fitting from search results
  const af = t.closest('[data-add-fit]');
  if (af) { const fid=af.dataset.addFit; const fit=FITTINGS.find(f=>f.id===fid); if(fit){SS.runs[SS.activeRun].steps.push({type:'fitting',fid:fid}); SS.searchTerm=''; renderRunArea(); calcSystem(); if(fit.branch){/* Could prompt for branch creation */}} return; }
  // Fitting info toggle
  const fi = t.closest('[data-fit-info]');
  if (fi) { const el=document.getElementById('fd-'+fi.dataset.fitInfo); if(el){el.style.display=el.style.display==='none'?'block':'none';} ev.stopPropagation(); return; }
  // Collar add
  if (t.closest('#addCollarBtn')) { const sz=document.getElementById('collarSizeSel').value; const tp=document.getElementById('collarTypeSel')?document.getElementById('collarTypeSel').value:'tab'; SS.collars.push({size:sz,type:tp}); renderCollars(); return; }
  // Collar remove
  const crm = t.closest('[data-col-rm]');
  if (crm) { SS.collars.splice(parseInt(crm.dataset.colRm),1); renderCollars(); return; }

  // Return collar add
  if (t.closest('#addRetCollarBtn')) { const sz=document.getElementById('retCollarSizeSel').value; const tp=document.getElementById('retCollarTypeSel')?document.getElementById('retCollarTypeSel').value:'tab'; SS.retCollars.push({size:sz,type:tp}); renderRetCollars();


 return; }
  // Return collar remove
  const rcrm = t.closest('[data-ret-col-rm]');
  if (rcrm) { SS.retCollars.splice(parseInt(rcrm.dataset.retColRm),1); renderRetCollars();


 return; }
  // Section toggle
  const tog = t.closest('[data-sys-toggle]');
  if (tog) { const key=tog.dataset.sysToggle; const bodies={plenum:'sysPlBody',retplenum:'sysRetPlBody',cfmest:'cfmEstBody',branchtree:'branchTreeBody'}; const b=document.getElementById(bodies[key]); if(b){b.classList.toggle('collapsed');tog.classList.toggle('collapsed');} return; }
  // Go to run from summary
  const go = t.closest('[data-goto]');
  if (go) { saveRunFromDOM(); SS.activeRun=parseInt(go.dataset.goto); SS.addMode=null; renderRunArea(); calcSystem(); document.getElementById('sysRunArea').scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth'}); return; }
  // CFM remove room
  const cfmrm = t.closest('[data-cfm-rm]');
  if (cfmrm) { cfmRooms.splice(parseInt(cfmrm.dataset.cfmRm),1); renderCfmEst(); return; }
  // CFM add room
  // Tightness selector
  const tb=t.closest('[data-tightness]');
  if(tb){cfmEstTightness=tb.dataset.tightness;renderCfmEst();return;}
  const eb=t.closest('[data-envelope]');
  if(eb){cfmEstEnvelope=eb.dataset.envelope;renderCfmEst();return;}
  const dl=t.closest('[data-ductloc]');
  if(dl){cfmEstDuctLoc=dl.dataset.ductloc;renderCfmEst();return;}
  if (t.closest('#cfmAddRoom')) { cfmRooms.push({name:'Room '+(cfmRooms.length+1),sqft:150,ceilHt:8,roomType:'bedroom'}); renderCfmEst(); return; }
});

// Input events
document.getElementById('page-system').addEventListener('input', function(ev) {
  if (typeof wizHandleChange === 'function' && wizHandleChange(ev)) return;
  const t = ev.target;
  if (t.id==='sysDSize'){SS.runs[SS.activeRun].ductSize=parseInt(t.value)||8;calcSystem();return;}
  if (t.id==='sysASP'){SS.runs[SS.activeRun].asp=parseFloat(t.value)||0.50;calcSystem();return;}
  if (t.id==='mjTarget'){calcSystem();return;}
  if (t.id==='fitSearch'){SS.searchTerm=t.value;const res=document.getElementById('fitResults');if(res)res.innerHTML=renderFittingResults();return;}
  // CFM room name
  const cn=t.closest('[data-cfm-name]');
  if(cn){cfmRooms[parseInt(cn.dataset.cfmName)].name=cn.value;return;}
  const ct=t.closest('[data-cfm-type]');
  if(ct){cfmRooms[parseInt(ct.dataset.cfmType)].roomType=ct.value;renderCfmEst();return;}
  // CFM sqft
  const cs=t.closest('[data-cfm-sqft]');
  if(cs){cfmRooms[parseInt(cs.dataset.cfmSqft)].sqft=parseFloat(cs.value)||0;renderCfmEst();return;}
  // CFM ceiling height
  const ch=t.closest('[data-cfm-ht]');
  if(ch){cfmRooms[parseInt(ch.dataset.cfmHt)].ceilHt=parseFloat(ch.value)||8;renderCfmEst();return;}
});

document.getElementById('page-system').addEventListener('change', function(ev) {
  if (typeof wizHandleChange === 'function' && wizHandleChange(ev)) return;
  if (ev.target.id==='sysDSize'){SS.runs[SS.activeRun].ductSize=parseInt(ev.target.value)||8;calcSystem();}
  var ct2=ev.target.closest('[data-cfm-type]');
  if(ct2){cfmRooms[parseInt(ct2.dataset.cfmType)].roomType=ct2.value;renderCfmEst();}
});

function saveRunFromDOM() {
  const r = SS.runs[SS.activeRun];
  if (!r) return;
  const ds = document.getElementById('sysDSize');
  const asp = document.getElementById('sysASP');
  if (ds) r.ductSize = parseInt(ds.value)||8;
  if (asp) r.asp = parseFloat(asp.value)||0.50;
}


// ===== RETURN PLENUM FILTER LOGIC =====
var sysRetFilterState = {
  enabled: false,
  mfg: 'generic',
  model: '4in-M11',
  grille: '20x20',
  cfm: 1200,
  filterPD: 0,
  faceVel: 0
};

function initSysRetFilterModels() {
  var modelSel = document.getElementById('sysRetFilterModel');
  if (!modelSel) return;
  var models = FILTER_DB[sysRetFilterState.mfg] || [];
  modelSel.innerHTML = models.map(function(m) {
    return '<option value="' + m.model + '">' + m.name + '</option>';
  }).join('');
  if (models.length > 0) sysRetFilterState.model = models[0].model;
  calcSysRetFilter();
}

function calcSysRetFilter() {
  var toggle = document.getElementById('sysRetFilterToggle');
  var configDiv = document.getElementById('sysRetFilterConfig');
  var resultsDiv = document.getElementById('sysRetFilterResults');
  var warnDiv = document.getElementById('sysRetFilterWarn');
  var impactDiv = document.getElementById('sysRetFilterImpact');
  if (!toggle || !configDiv) return;
  
  sysRetFilterState.enabled = toggle.checked;
  configDiv.style.display = toggle.checked ? '' : 'none';
  
  if (!toggle.checked) {
    sysRetFilterState.filterPD = 0;
    sysRetFilterState.faceVel = 0;
    if (resultsDiv) resultsDiv.innerHTML = '';
    if (warnDiv) { warnDiv.style.display = 'none'; warnDiv.innerHTML = ''; }
    if (impactDiv) impactDiv.style.display = 'none';
    return;
  }
  
  var mfg = document.getElementById('sysRetFilterMfg').value;
  var modelId = document.getElementById('sysRetFilterModel').value;
  var grille = document.getElementById('sysRetFilterGrille').value;
  var sysCFM = parseFloat(document.getElementById('sysRetFilterCFM').value) || 1200;
  
  sysRetFilterState.mfg = mfg;
  sysRetFilterState.model = modelId;
  sysRetFilterState.grille = grille;
  sysRetFilterState.cfm = sysCFM;
  
  var models = FILTER_DB[mfg] || [];
  var filt = models.find(function(m) { return m.model === modelId; });
  if (!filt) return;
  
  // Face velocity
  var gParts = grille.split('x');
  var gArea = (parseInt(gParts[0]) * parseInt(gParts[1])) / 144;
  var faceVel = sysCFM / gArea;
  
  // PD scaled by square law
  var ratio = sysCFM / filt.ratedCfm;
  var pd = filt.ratedPD * ratio * ratio;
  
  sysRetFilterState.filterPD = pd;
  sysRetFilterState.faceVel = faceVel;
  
  var fvClass = faceVel > 500 ? 'danger' : (faceVel > 400 ? 'warn' : 'ok');
  var pdClass = pd > 0.25 ? 'danger' : (pd > 0.15 ? 'warn' : 'ok');
  
  if (resultsDiv) {
    resultsDiv.innerHTML = 
      '<div class="filter-inline-stat"><div class="filter-inline-stat-val ' + fvClass + '">' + Math.round(faceVel) + '</div><div class="filter-inline-stat-label">Face Vel (FPM)</div></div>' +
      '<div class="filter-inline-stat"><div class="filter-inline-stat-val ' + pdClass + '">' + pd.toFixed(2) + '</div><div class="filter-inline-stat-label">Filter PD (IWC)</div></div>' +
      '<div class="filter-inline-stat"><div class="filter-inline-stat-val">' + filt.merv + '</div><div class="filter-inline-stat-label">MERV Rating</div></div>' +
      '<div class="filter-inline-stat"><div class="filter-inline-stat-val">' + filt.depth + '"</div><div class="filter-inline-stat-label">Filter Depth</div></div>';
  }
  
  // Warnings
  var warns = [];
  if (faceVel > 500) warns.push('<strong>\u26a0 Face velocity ' + Math.round(faceVel) + ' FPM exceeds 500 FPM max.</strong> Increase filter grille size or add a second return.');
  if (faceVel > 300 && faceVel <= 500) warns.push('Face velocity ' + Math.round(faceVel) + ' FPM is within ASHRAE 52.2 test range (300\u2013492 FPM).');
  if (pd > 0.30) warns.push('Filter PD ' + pd.toFixed(2) + ' IWC is very high. Consider lower MERV or deeper media.');
  
  if (warns.length > 0 && warnDiv) {
    var warnClass = faceVel > 500 ? 'danger' : '';
    warnDiv.style.display = '';
    warnDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="filter-warning-banner ' + warnClass + '" style="margin-top:8px"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" width="14" height="14"><path d="M10.29 3.86L1.82 18a2 2 0 001.71 3h16.94a2 2 0 001.71-3L13.71 3.86a2 2 0 00-3.42 0z"/><line x1="12" y1="9" x2="12" y2="13"/><line x1="12" y1="17" x2="12.01" y2="17"/></svg><span>' + warns.join('<br>') + '</span></div>';
  } else if (warnDiv) {
    warnDiv.style.display = 'none';
  }
  
  // System impact — show how filter eats into ASP
  if (impactDiv) {
    impactDiv.style.display = '';
    // Get a representative ASP from runs (use first return run, or first run)
    var asp = 0.50;
    SS.runs.forEach(function(r) { if (r.airPath === 'return' && r.asp > 0) asp = r.asp; });
    if (asp === 0.50) SS.runs.forEach(function(r) { if (r.asp > 0) asp = r.asp; });
    
    var effASP = Math.max(0, asp - pd);
    // Suggested FR for return = effASP / estimated longest return TEL * 100
    var longestRetTEL = 0;
    SS.runs.forEach(function(r) { if (r.airPath === 'return' && r.totalTEL > longestRetTEL) longestRetTEL = r.totalTEL; });
    var sugFR = longestRetTEL > 0 ? ((effASP / longestRetTEL) * 100).toFixed(3) : '--';
    
    document.getElementById('sysRetFiltPD').textContent = pd.toFixed(2) + ' IWC';
    document.getElementById('sysRetFiltPD').style.color = pd > 0.25 ? 'var(--red-glow)' : 'var(--text)';
    
    var velEl = document.getElementById('sysRetFiltVel');
    velEl.textContent = Math.round(faceVel) + ' FPM';
    velEl.className = 'filter-impact-value ' + fvClass;
    
    document.getElementById('sysRetTotalASP').textContent = asp.toFixed(2) + ' IWC';
    
    var effEl = document.getElementById('sysRetEffASP');
    effEl.textContent = effASP.toFixed(2) + ' IWC';
    effEl.style.color = effASP < 0.15 ? 'var(--red-glow)' : (effASP < 0.25 ? 'var(--yellow)' : 'var(--green)');
    
    document.getElementById('sysRetSugFR').textContent = sugFR === '--' ? sugFR : sugFR + ' IWC/100ft';
  }
}

// ===== SYSTEM FILTER EVENT DELEGATION =====
(function() {
  var sysPage = document.getElementById('page-system');
  if (!sysPage) return;
  
  sysPage.addEventListener('change', function(ev) {
    if (typeof wizHandleChange === 'function' && wizHandleChange(ev)) return;
    var t = ev.target;
    // Filter toggle
    if (t.dataset.sysFilterToggle !== undefined) {
      var ri = parseInt(t.dataset.sysFilterToggle);
      SS.runs[ri].hasFilter = t.checked;
      var cfg = document.querySelector('[data-sys-filter-config="'+ri+'"]');
      if (cfg) cfg.style.display = t.checked ? '' : 'none';
      saveRunFromDOM();
      calcSystem();
      return;
    }
    // Filter manufacturer
    if (t.dataset.sysFilterMfg !== undefined) {
      var ri2 = parseInt(t.dataset.sysFilterMfg);
      SS.runs[ri2].filterMfg = t.value;
      // Repopulate model dropdown
      var modelSel = document.querySelector('[data-sys-filter-model="'+ri2+'"]');
      if (modelSel) {
        var models = FILTER_DB[t.value] || [];
        modelSel.innerHTML = models.map(function(m) {
          return '<option value="' + m.model + '">' + m.name + '</option>';
        }).join('');
        if (models.length) SS.runs[ri2].filterModel = models[0].model;
      }
      saveRunFromDOM();
      calcSystem();
      return;
    }
    // Filter model
    if (t.dataset.sysFilterModel !== undefined) {
      var ri3 = parseInt(t.dataset.sysFilterModel);
      SS.runs[ri3].filterModel = t.value;
      saveRunFromDOM();
      calcSystem();
      return;
    }
    // Filter grille size
    if (t.dataset.sysFilterGrille !== undefined) {
      var ri4 = parseInt(t.dataset.sysFilterGrille);
      SS.runs[ri4].filterGrille = t.value;
      saveRunFromDOM();
      calcSystem();
      return;
    }
  });
})();

// ===== FRICTION RATE WORKSHEET =====
function calcFrictionRate() {
  // Step 1: ESP
  const esp = parseFloat(document.getElementById('frESP').value) || 0;
  const blowerCfm = parseFloat(document.getElementById('frCFM').value) || 0;

  // Step 2: Sum all CPL inputs
  const cplIds = ['frCPL_dxCoil','frCPL_elecCoil','frCPL_hwCoil','frCPL_heatExch',
    'frCPL_loFilter','frCPL_hiFilter','frCPL_elecFilter','frCPL_humid',
    'frCPL_supplyOut','frCPL_returnGrille','frCPL_damper','frCPL_other'];
  let cpl = 0;
  cplIds.forEach(id => { cpl += parseFloat(document.getElementById(id).value) || 0; });
  document.getElementById('frCPLTotal').textContent = cpl.toFixed(2);

  // Step 3: ASP
  const asp = Math.max(esp - cpl, 0);
  document.getElementById('frASP_esp').textContent = esp.toFixed(2);
  document.getElementById('frASP_cpl').textContent = cpl.toFixed(2);
  document.getElementById('frASP').textContent = asp.toFixed(2);

  // Step 4: TEL
  const telSup = parseFloat(document.getElementById('frTEL_supply').value) || 0;
  const telRet = parseFloat(document.getElementById('frTEL_return').value) || 0;
  const tel = telSup + telRet;
  document.getElementById('frTEL_supVal').textContent = Math.round(telSup);
  document.getElementById('frTEL_retVal').textContent = Math.round(telRet);
  document.getElementById('frTEL').textContent = Math.round(tel);

  // Step 5: Friction Rate
  let fr = 0;
  if (tel > 0) fr = (asp * 100) / tel;
  document.getElementById('frFR_asp').textContent = asp.toFixed(2);
  document.getElementById('frFR_tel').textContent = Math.round(tel);
  document.getElementById('frFR').textContent = fr.toFixed(3);

  // Result card
  const card = document.getElementById('frResultCard');
  const title = document.getElementById('frResultTitle');
  const msg = document.getElementById('frResultMsg');

  title.textContent = 'FRICTION RATE: ' + fr.toFixed(3) + ' IWC/100ft';

  if (tel === 0 || esp === 0) {
    card.className = 'fr-result-card fr-result-warn';
    msg.textContent = 'Enter your equipment ESP and total effective length to calculate the design friction rate.';
  } else if (fr < 0.06) {
    card.className = 'fr-result-card fr-result-warn';
    msg.textContent = 'Below the ACCA recommended 0.06\u20130.18 range. Fan may be undersized for duct system. Consider: increasing blower speed, reducing TEL, or selecting a higher-ESP unit.';
  } else if (fr > 0.18) {
    card.className = 'fr-result-card fr-result-bad';
    msg.textContent = 'Above the ACCA recommended 0.06\u20130.18 range. Fan may be too powerful or duct system too short. Consider: decreasing blower speed, increasing TEL, or checking for excessive air velocity.';
  } else {
    card.className = 'fr-result-card fr-result-ok';
    msg.textContent = 'Within the ACCA recommended 0.06\u20130.18 range. This friction rate is acceptable for duct sizing.';
  }

  // Heating / Cooling factors
  const heatLoss = parseFloat(document.getElementById('frHeatLoss').value) || 0;
  const sensGain = parseFloat(document.getElementById('frSensGain').value) || 0;
  document.getElementById('frHF').textContent = heatLoss > 0 ? (blowerCfm / heatLoss).toFixed(4) : '\u2014';
  document.getElementById('frCF').textContent = sensGain > 0 ? (blowerCfm / sensGain).toFixed(4) : '\u2014';

  // Draw chart
  drawFrictionRateChart(asp, tel, fr);
}

function drawFrictionRateChart(asp, tel, fr) {
  const canvas = document.getElementById('frChart');
  if (!canvas) return;
  const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
  const w = 340, h = 280;
  canvas.width = w * dpr;
  canvas.height = h * dpr;
  canvas.style.width = w + 'px';
  canvas.style.height = h + 'px';
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
  ctx.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);

  // Chart area
  const left = 50, right = w - 20, top = 20, bottom = h - 40;
  const cw = right - left, ch = bottom - top;

  // Scales: ASP 0.05 to 0.40, TEL 50 to 500
  const aspMin = 0.05, aspMax = 0.40;
  const telMin = 50, telMax = 500;

  function xPos(a) { return left + ((a - aspMin) / (aspMax - aspMin)) * cw; }
  function yPos(t) { return bottom - ((t - telMin) / (telMax - telMin)) * ch; }

  // Grid
  ctx.strokeStyle = '#333';
  ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
  const aspTicks = [0.05, 0.10, 0.15, 0.20, 0.25, 0.30, 0.35, 0.40];
  const telTicks = [50, 100, 150, 200, 250, 300, 350, 400, 450, 500];
  aspTicks.forEach(a => {
    const x = xPos(a);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(x, top); ctx.lineTo(x, bottom); ctx.stroke();
  });
  telTicks.forEach(t => {
    const y = yPos(t);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(left, y); ctx.lineTo(right, y); ctx.stroke();
  });

  // ACCA wedge (0.06 to 0.18 lines)
  const frLines = [0.06, 0.08, 0.10, 0.12, 0.14, 0.18];
  const frColors = ['#4CAF50','#66BB6A','#8BC34A','#CDDC39','#FFC107','#FF9800'];
  frLines.forEach((frVal, i) => {
    ctx.strokeStyle = frColors[i];
    ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
    ctx.setLineDash([4, 3]);
    ctx.beginPath();
    let started = false;
    for (let a = aspMin; a <= aspMax; a += 0.005) {
      const t = (a * 100) / frVal;
      if (t < telMin || t > telMax) continue;
      const x = xPos(a), y = yPos(t);
      if (!started) { ctx.moveTo(x, y); started = true; } else { ctx.lineTo(x, y); }
    }
    ctx.stroke();
    ctx.setLineDash([]);
    // Label
    const labelA = Math.min(frVal * telMax / 100, aspMax);
    const labelT = (labelA * 100) / frVal;
    if (labelT >= telMin && labelT <= telMax && labelA >= aspMin) {
      ctx.fillStyle = frColors[i];
      ctx.font = '10px Inter, sans-serif';
      ctx.fillText(frVal.toFixed(2), xPos(labelA) + 3, yPos(labelT) - 4);
    }
  });

  // Wedge fill (between 0.06 and 0.18)
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(76, 175, 80, 0.06)';
  ctx.beginPath();
  // Bottom line (0.18) left to right
  let pts06 = [], pts18 = [];
  for (let a = aspMin; a <= aspMax; a += 0.005) {
    const t06 = (a * 100) / 0.06, t18 = (a * 100) / 0.18;
    if (t06 >= telMin && t06 <= telMax) pts06.push({x: xPos(a), y: yPos(t06)});
    if (t18 >= telMin && t18 <= telMax) pts18.push({x: xPos(a), y: yPos(t18)});
  }
  if (pts18.length > 0 && pts06.length > 0) {
    ctx.beginPath();
    pts06.forEach((p, i) => i === 0 ? ctx.moveTo(p.x, p.y) : ctx.lineTo(p.x, p.y));
    for (let i = pts18.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) ctx.lineTo(pts18[i].x, pts18[i].y);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.fill();
  }

  // Axes
  ctx.strokeStyle = '#666';
  ctx.lineWidth = 1;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(left, top); ctx.lineTo(left, bottom); ctx.lineTo(right, bottom);
  ctx.stroke();

  // Axis labels
  ctx.fillStyle = '#999';
  ctx.font = '10px Inter, sans-serif';
  ctx.textAlign = 'center';
  aspTicks.forEach(a => {
    ctx.fillText(a.toFixed(2), xPos(a), bottom + 14);
  });
  ctx.fillText('Available Static Pressure (IWC)', (left + right) / 2, bottom + 30);

  ctx.textAlign = 'right';
  telTicks.forEach(t => {
    ctx.fillText(t, left - 6, yPos(t) + 3);
  });
  ctx.save();
  ctx.translate(12, (top + bottom) / 2);
  ctx.rotate(-Math.PI / 2);
  ctx.textAlign = 'center';
  ctx.fillText('TEL (ft)', 0, 0);
  ctx.restore();

  // Plot the current point
  if (asp >= aspMin && asp <= aspMax && tel >= telMin && tel <= telMax) {
    const px = xPos(asp), py = yPos(tel);
    // Crosshairs
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(211, 47, 47, 0.4)';
    ctx.lineWidth = 1;
    ctx.setLineDash([3, 3]);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(px, bottom); ctx.lineTo(px, py); ctx.stroke();
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(left, py); ctx.lineTo(px, py); ctx.stroke();
    ctx.setLineDash([]);
    // Dot
    ctx.fillStyle = '#D32F2F';
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(px, py, 5, 0, Math.PI * 2); ctx.fill();
    ctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(px, py, 2, 0, Math.PI * 2); ctx.fill();
    // FR label at point
    ctx.fillStyle = '#F0F0F0';
    ctx.font = 'bold 11px JetBrains Mono, monospace';
    ctx.textAlign = 'left';
    ctx.fillText('FR=' + fr.toFixed(3), px + 8, py - 6);
  }
}

// ===== EVENT LISTENERS (no inline handlers for CSP compatibility) =====

// Nav tabs
document.querySelectorAll('.nav-tab[data-page]').forEach(btn => {
  btn.addEventListener('click', () => showPage(btn.dataset.page));
});

// Round size slider + input sync
var ROUND_SIZES = [4,5,6,7,8,9,10,12,14,16,18,20,22,24];
var roundSizeSlider = document.getElementById('roundSizeSlider');
var roundSizeVal = document.getElementById('roundSizeVal');
if (roundSizeSlider && roundSizeVal) {
  roundSizeSlider.addEventListener('input', function() {
    var idx = parseInt(roundSizeSlider.value);
    roundSizeVal.value = ROUND_SIZES[idx];
    calculate();
  });
  roundSizeVal.addEventListener('input', function() {
    var v = parseInt(roundSizeVal.value) || 10;
    // Find closest size in array
    var closest = 0;
    for (var i = 0; i < ROUND_SIZES.length; i++) {
      if (Math.abs(ROUND_SIZES[i] - v) < Math.abs(ROUND_SIZES[closest] - v)) closest = i;
    }
    roundSizeSlider.value = closest;
    calculate();
  });
}

      if (Math.abs(RECT_W_SIZES[i] - v) < Math.abs(RECT_W_SIZES[closest] - v)) closest = i;

  });
}

  { id:'reducer', name:'Reducer',        eqFn: function(){ return 5; } }
];

// Filter grill PD lookup: [depth][merv] = PD at 1000 CFM rated
var FILTER_GRILL_PD = {
  '1': { '6': 0.08, '8': 0.12, '11': 0.18, '13': 0.25 },
  '2': { '6': 0.05, '8': 0.08, '11': 0.12, '13': 0.17 },
  '4': { '6': 0.03, '8': 0.05, '11': 0.08, '13': 0.11 }
};

var FILTER_GRILL_SIZES = ['12x12','14x20','14x25','16x16','16x20','16x25','20x20','20x25','20x30','24x24','25x16','25x20','30x20'];

function wizCalcFilterGrillPD(br) {
  if (!br.hasFilterGrill) return 0;
  var depth = String(br.filterDepth || '1');
  var merv = String(br.grillMerv || '8');
  var grillSize = br.grillSize || '20x20';
  var parts = grillSize.split('x');
  var w = parseFloat(parts[0]) || 20;
  var h = parseFloat(parts[1]) || 20;
  var faceArea = (w * h) / 144; // sq ft
  var cfm = parseFloat(br.cfm) || 0;
  if (cfm <= 0 || faceArea <= 0) return 0;
  var faceVel = cfm / faceArea;
  // Grille PD (stamped face, ~0.02 at 300 FPM, scales with square law)
  var grillePD = 0.02 * Math.pow(faceVel / 300, 2);
  // Filter PD scaled from 1000 CFM rated
  var ratedPD = (FILTER_GRILL_PD[depth] && FILTER_GRILL_PD[depth][merv]) || 0.12;
  var filterPD = ratedPD * Math.pow(cfm / 1000, 2);
  return grillePD + filterPD;
}

// ---- helpers ----
function wizFlexFactor(c) {
  c = c || 0;
  if (c <= 0)  return 1;
  if (c <= 15) return 1 + (c / 15);
  return 2 + ((c - 15) / 15) * 2;
}

function wizRectEqDia(w, h) {
  w = parseFloat(w) || 1;
  h = parseFloat(h) || 1;
  return 1.3 * Math.pow(w * h, 0.625) / Math.pow(w + h, 0.25);
}

function wizEffDia(obj) {
  if (!obj) return 6;
  if (obj.shape === 'rect') return wizRectEqDia(obj.width || 8, obj.height || 8);
  return parseFloat(obj.size) || 6;
}

function wizSizeLabel(obj) {
  if (!obj) return '';
  if (obj.isRadial) return 'Plenum';
  if (obj.shape === 'rect') return (obj.width || '?') + '\u00D7' + (obj.height || '?') + '"';
  return (obj.size || '?') + '\u2033';
}
