// ---- SVG illustrations for boots, takeoffs, fittings ----
function wizBootSVG(type, position) {
  var dc = '#d32f2f'; // duct walls
  var ac = '#4caf50'; // airflow
  var lc = '#888';    // labels
  var s = '<svg viewBox="0 0 120 80" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">';
  if (type === 'straightboot' && position === 'floor') {
    s += '<rect x="35" y="5" width="50" height="35" rx="3" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<rect x="40" y="40" width="40" height="25" rx="2" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<rect x="35" y="65" width="50" height="10" rx="2" fill="' + lc + '" opacity=".2" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="1"/>';
    s += '<path d="M60 15 L60 55" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="4 2" marker-end="url(#arrowG)"/>';
  } else if (type === 'straightboot' && position === 'ceiling') {
    s += '<rect x="35" y="5" width="50" height="10" rx="2" fill="' + lc + '" opacity=".2" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="1"/>';
    s += '<rect x="40" y="15" width="40" height="25" rx="2" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<rect x="35" y="40" width="50" height="35" rx="3" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<path d="M60 65 L60 25" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="4 2" marker-end="url(#arrowG)"/>';
  } else if (type === '90boot' || type === '90deg') {
    s += '<rect x="10" y="20" width="50" height="24" rx="3" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<rect x="60" y="20" width="24" height="45" rx="3" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<rect x="55" y="65" width="34" height="10" rx="2" fill="' + lc + '" opacity=".2" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="1"/>';
    s += '<path d="M20 32 L55 32 Q65 32 65 42 L65 55" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="4 2" marker-end="url(#arrowG)"/>';
  } else if (type === 'register') {
    s += '<rect x="25" y="10" width="70" height="20" rx="3" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<rect x="30" y="30" width="60" height="40" rx="4" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<line x1="42" y1="34" x2="42" y2="66" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="1"/>';
    s += '<line x1="54" y1="34" x2="54" y2="66" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="1"/>';

    s += '<line x1="78" y1="34" x2="78" y2="66" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="1"/>';
  } else if (type === '45deg' || type === '45boot') {
    s += '<rect x="10" y="15" width="45" height="22" rx="3" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<path d="M55 15 L90 45 L90 70 L55 37 Z" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';

    s += '<path d="M20 26 L55 26 L82 52" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="4 2" marker-end="url(#arrowG)"/>';
  } else if (type === 'transition') {
    s += '<rect x="15" y="15" width="40" height="28" rx="3" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';

  } else {
    // Default: straight90
    s += '<rect x="5" y="28" width="110" height="24" rx="4" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<rect x="50" y="5" width="20" height="23" rx="2" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<path d="M60 25 L60 8" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="4 2" marker-end="url(#arrowT)"/>';
  }
  s += '<defs><marker id="arrowT" viewBox="0 0 10 10" refX="9" refY="5" markerWidth="6" markerHeight="6" orient="auto"><path d="M0 0 L10 5 L0 10 z" fill="' + ac + '"/></marker></defs>';
  s += '</svg>';
  return s;
}

function wizFittingSVG(type) {
  var dc = '#d32f2f';
  var ac = '#4caf50';
  var s = '<svg viewBox="0 0 120 80" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">';
  if (type === 'elbow90') {
    s += '<path d="M15 70 L15 35 Q15 15 35 15 L70 15" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="3" fill="none" stroke-linecap="round"/>';
    s += '<path d="M25 70 L25 40 Q25 25 40 25 L70 25" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="3" fill="none" stroke-linecap="round"/>';
    s += '<path d="M20 65 L20 38 Q20 20 38 20 L65 20" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="4 2" marker-end="url(#arrowF)"/>';
  } else if (type === 'elbow45') {
    s += '<path d="M15 65 L15 40 L55 15" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="3" fill="none" stroke-linecap="round"/>';
    s += '<path d="M25 65 L25 45 L65 20" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="3" fill="none" stroke-linecap="round"/>';
    s += '<path d="M20 60 L20 42 L58 18" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="4 2" marker-end="url(#arrowF)"/>';
  } else if (type === 'tee') {
    s += '<rect x="10" y="30" width="100" height="20" rx="3" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<rect x="50" y="5" width="20" height="25" rx="2" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<path d="M20 40 L45 40" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="4 2"/>';
    s += '<path d="M75 40 L100 40" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="4 2" marker-end="url(#arrowF)"/>';
    s += '<path d="M60 27 L60 10" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="4 2" marker-end="url(#arrowF)"/>';
  } else if (type === 'wye') {
    s += '<rect x="5" y="35" width="45" height="16" rx="3" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<path d="M50 35 L85 18 L90 22 L57 39" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<path d="M50 51 L85 62 L90 58 L57 47" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<path d="M15 43 L50 43" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="4 2"/>';
    s += '<path d="M52 40 L80 22" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="4 2" marker-end="url(#arrowF)"/>';
    s += '<path d="M52 46 L80 58" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="4 2" marker-end="url(#arrowF)"/>';
  } else if (type === 'reducer') {
    s += '<path d="M10 25 L50 30 L110 30 L110 50 L50 50 L10 55 Z" stroke="' + dc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<path d="M20 40 L100 40" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="4 2" marker-end="url(#arrowF)"/>';
  } else {
    return '';
  }
  s += '<defs><marker id="arrowF" viewBox="0 0 10 10" refX="9" refY="5" markerWidth="6" markerHeight="6" orient="auto"><path d="M0 0 L10 5 L0 10 z" fill="' + ac + '"/></marker></defs>';
  s += '</svg>';
  return s;
}

// ---- Plenum SVG illustrations ----
// Supply: closed ends, air exits through SIDE takeoff collars only
// Return: air flows FROM return ducts TOWARD the AHU
function wizPlenumSVG(type, isReturn) {
  var wc = isReturn ? '#ff9800' : '#d32f2f'; // duct wall color
  var ac = '#4caf50'; // airflow
  var bg = '#333';    // AHU box fill
  var lc = '#888';    // labels/structure
  var s = '<svg viewBox="0 0 220 140" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">';

  // =============== SUPPLY PLENUMS ===============
  // Orientation: AHU at bottom, plenum on top, air goes UP from AHU
  // then TURNS SIDEWAYS to exit through side collars (left and right)
  // End cap is on TOP (closed) — air cannot exit the end

  if (type === 'tapered') {
    // AHU box at bottom center
    s += '<rect x="75" y="95" width="70" height="35" rx="4" fill="' + bg + '" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<text x="110" y="117" text-anchor="middle" font-size="9" fill="#aaa">AHU</text>';
    // Tapered plenum on top
    s += '<path d="M65 95 L65 40 L85 20 L135 20 L155 40 L155 95 Z" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<line x1="85" y1="20" x2="135" y2="20" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="3"/>';
    // Side collars
    s += '<rect x="155" y="38" width="22" height="14" rx="6" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<rect x="43" y="38" width="22" height="14" rx="6" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<rect x="155" y="62" width="22" height="14" rx="6" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    if (isReturn) {
      // RETURN: Air comes IN from side collars, flows DOWN into AHU
      s += '<line x1="110" y1="55" x2="110" y2="93" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="106,88 110,96 114,88" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
      // Arrows: FROM collars INTO plenum
      s += '<line x1="175" y1="45" x2="157" y2="45" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="159,49 153,45 159,41" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
      s += '<line x1="47" y1="45" x2="63" y2="45" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="61,41 67,45 61,49" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
      s += '<line x1="175" y1="69" x2="157" y2="69" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="159,73 153,69 159,65" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    } else {
      // SUPPLY: Air goes UP from AHU, turns sideways OUT collars
      s += '<line x1="110" y1="93" x2="110" y2="55" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="106,58 110,48 114,58" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
      s += '<line x1="155" y1="45" x2="175" y2="45" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="173,41 181,45 173,49" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
      s += '<line x1="65" y1="45" x2="47" y2="45" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="49,49 41,45 49,41" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
      s += '<line x1="155" y1="69" x2="175" y2="69" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="173,65 181,69 173,73" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    }
    s += '<text x="110" y="137" text-anchor="middle" font-size="7" fill="' + lc + '">Tapered Transition \u2014 10ft EQ (Best)</text>';
  } else if (type === 'box') {
    // AHU at bottom
    s += '<rect x="75" y="95" width="70" height="35" rx="4" fill="' + bg + '" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<text x="110" y="117" text-anchor="middle" font-size="9" fill="#aaa">AHU</text>';
    // Box plenum on top — rectangular, closed top
    s += '<rect x="60" y="20" width="100" height="75" rx="3" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    // Closed top
    s += '<line x1="60" y1="20" x2="160" y2="20" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="3"/>';
    // Side collars
    s += '<rect x="160" y="35" width="22" height="14" rx="6" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<rect x="160" y="60" width="22" height="14" rx="6" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<rect x="38" y="45" width="22" height="14" rx="6" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    // Turbulence at 90° turn
    s += '<circle cx="95" cy="55" r="4" stroke="#d32f2f" stroke-width="1" fill="none" opacity=".4"/>';
    s += '<circle cx="120" cy="45" r="3" stroke="#d32f2f" stroke-width="1" fill="none" opacity=".35"/>';
    s += '<circle cx="105" cy="70" r="3.5" stroke="#d32f2f" stroke-width="1" fill="none" opacity=".3"/>';
    if (isReturn) {
      // RETURN: Air comes IN from side collars, flows DOWN into AHU
      s += '<line x1="110" y1="50" x2="110" y2="93" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="106,88 110,96 114,88" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
      // FROM right collars INTO plenum
      s += '<line x1="180" y1="42" x2="162" y2="42" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="164,46 158,42 164,38" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
      s += '<line x1="180" y1="67" x2="162" y2="67" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="164,71 158,67 164,63" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
      // FROM left collar INTO plenum
      s += '<line x1="42" y1="52" x2="58" y2="52" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="56,48 62,52 56,56" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    } else {
      // SUPPLY: Air goes UP, turns sideways OUT collars

      s += '<polygon points="178,38 186,42 178,46" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
      s += '<line x1="160" y1="67" x2="180" y2="67" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="178,63 186,67 178,71" fill="' + ac + '"/>';

    }
    s += '<text x="110" y="137" text-anchor="middle" font-size="7" fill="' + lc + '">Box Plenum \u2014 35ft EQ</text>';
  } else if (type === 'extended') {
    // Extended plenum: AHU at left, long horizontal plenum extending right
    // Multiple collars along the top coming off at intervals
    s += '<rect x="5" y="50" width="40" height="50" rx="4" fill="' + bg + '" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<text x="25" y="80" text-anchor="middle" font-size="8" fill="#aaa">AHU</text>';
    // Long horizontal plenum — closed at far end
    s += '<rect x="45" y="50" width="165" height="30" rx="3" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    // Closed end cap at right
    s += '<line x1="210" y1="50" x2="210" y2="80" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="3"/>';
    // Takeoff collars along TOP
    s += '<rect x="62" y="30" width="14" height="20" rx="6" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<rect x="92" y="30" width="14" height="20" rx="6" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<rect x="122" y="30" width="14" height="20" rx="6" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<rect x="152" y="30" width="14" height="20" rx="6" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<rect x="182" y="30" width="14" height="20" rx="6" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    var cols = [69,99,129,159,189];
    if (isReturn) {
      // RETURN: Air comes DOWN from collars into plenum, flows LEFT toward AHU
      for (var ci=0; ci<cols.length; ci++) {

      // SUPPLY: Air enters from AHU horizontally, distributes out collars

      }
    }
    s += '<text x="120" y="100" text-anchor="middle" font-size="7" fill="' + lc + '">Extended Plenum \u2014 15ft EQ</text>';
  } else if (type === '90_vanes') {
    // 90deg turn with turning vanes
    s += '<rect x="5" y="50" width="40" height="50" rx="4" fill="' + bg + '" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';

    s += '<rect x="45" y="40" width="50" height="60" rx="3" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';

    s += '<path d="M65 95 Q65 55 80 42" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<rect x="85" y="12" width="30" height="16" rx="6" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    if (isReturn) {
      // RETURN: Air comes IN from collar, through vanes, toward AHU

      s += '<polygon points="50,79 42,75 50,71" fill="' + ac + '"/>';

      s += '<line x1="85" y1="20" x2="110" y2="20" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="110,16 118,20 110,24" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    }
    s += '<text x="140" y="75" font-size="7" fill="' + lc + '">20ft EQ</text>';
  } else if (type === '90_radius') {
    // 90deg radius bend
    s += '<rect x="5" y="50" width="40" height="50" rx="4" fill="' + bg + '" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';

    s += '<line x1="90" y1="10" x2="110" y2="10" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    if (isReturn) {
      // RETURN: Air comes IN from collar, curves down toward AHU

  } else if (type === 'bullhead') {
    // SUPPLY: AHU bottom center, T going left and right, closed at ends
    // AHU at bottom center
    s += '<rect x="80" y="82" width="40" height="30" rx="4" fill="' + bg + '" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';

    s += '<rect x="130" y="10" width="14" height="20" rx="6" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<rect x="160" y="10" width="14" height="20" rx="6" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    if (isReturn) {
      // RETURN: Air comes IN from collars, merges, flows DOWN to AHU
      var bCols = [32,62,137,167];
      for (var bci=0; bci<bCols.length; bci++) {
        s += '<line x1="'+bCols[bci]+'" y1="14" x2="'+bCols[bci]+'" y2="28" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';

      }
      s += '<line x1="40" y1="42" x2="100" y2="42" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
      s += '<line x1="160" y1="42" x2="100" y2="42" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
      s += '<line x1="100" y1="55" x2="100" y2="80" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="96,76 100,84 104,76" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    } else {
      // SUPPLY: Air goes UP from AHU, splits left/right, out collars
      s += '<line x1="100" y1="80" x2="100" y2="55" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
      s += '<line x1="100" y1="42" x2="40" y2="42" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
      s += '<line x1="100" y1="42" x2="160" y2="42" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
      var bCols = [32,62,137,167];
      for (var bci=0; bci<bCols.length; bci++) {
        s += '<line x1="'+bCols[bci]+'" y1="30" x2="'+bCols[bci]+'" y2="14" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
        s += '<polygon points="'+(bCols[bci]-4)+',14 '+bCols[bci]+',6 '+(bCols[bci]+4)+',14" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
      }
    }
    // Warning
    s += '<rect x="65" y="63" width="70" height="16" rx="4" fill="#d32f2f" opacity=".15" stroke="#d32f2f" stroke-width="1"/>';
    s += '<text x="100" y="74" text-anchor="middle" font-size="7" font-weight="bold" fill="#d32f2f">\u26A0 120ft EQ \u2014 Worst</text>';

  // ---- RETURN plenum types: air flows FROM ducts TOWARD AHU ----
  } else if (type === 'drop_90') {
    // RETURN: Right-angle drop, air comes from bottom, goes into AHU
    s += '<rect x="5" y="25" width="40" height="50" rx="4" fill="' + bg + '" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<text x="25" y="54" text-anchor="middle" font-size="9" fill="#aaa">AHU</text>';
    // Return box at top
    s += '<rect x="45" y="20" width="55" height="40" rx="3" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    // Return drop (vertical duct coming from below)
    s += '<rect x="62" y="60" width="20" height="45" rx="2" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    // Airflow: up from return duct INTO plenum TOWARD AHU
    s += '<line x1="72" y1="100" x2="72" y2="65" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<path d="M72 60 Q72 45 55 40" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="55,35 48,40 55,45" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    s += '<text x="130" y="80" font-size="7" fill="' + lc + '">65ft EQ</text>';
  } else if (type === 'drop_radius') {
    // RETURN: Drop with internal radius, air toward AHU
    s += '<rect x="5" y="25" width="40" height="50" rx="4" fill="' + bg + '" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<text x="25" y="54" text-anchor="middle" font-size="9" fill="#aaa">AHU</text>';
    // Return box
    s += '<rect x="45" y="20" width="55" height="40" rx="3" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    // Return drop with radius
    s += '<rect x="62" y="60" width="20" height="45" rx="2" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    // Internal radius guide
    s += '<path d="M78 60 Q78 45 62 38" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none" stroke-dasharray="4 2"/>';
    // Airflow: up with smooth curve toward AHU
    s += '<line x1="72" y1="100" x2="72" y2="70" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<path d="M72 65 Q72 48 55 42" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="55,37 48,42 55,47" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    s += '<text x="130" y="80" font-size="7" fill="' + lc + '">30ft EQ</text>';
  } else if (type === 'filter_rack') {
    // RETURN: Filter rack, air enters through filter toward AHU
    s += '<rect x="5" y="30" width="40" height="55" rx="4" fill="' + bg + '" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<text x="25" y="60" text-anchor="middle" font-size="9" fill="#aaa">AHU</text>';
    // Filter rack box
    s += '<rect x="45" y="25" width="50" height="65" rx="3" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    // Filter pattern (vertical lines)
    s += '<line x1="80" y1="30" x2="80" y2="85" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="1" stroke-dasharray="3 2"/>';
    s += '<line x1="85" y1="30" x2="85" y2="85" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="1" stroke-dasharray="3 2"/>';
    s += '<line x1="90" y1="30" x2="90" y2="85" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="1" stroke-dasharray="3 2"/>';
    // Return duct entering from right
    s += '<rect x="95" y="42" width="45" height="24" rx="3" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    // Airflow: from duct, through filter, toward AHU
    s += '<line x1="135" y1="54" x2="98" y2="54" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<line x1="75" y1="54" x2="48" y2="54" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="48,49 40,54 48,59" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    s += '<text x="155" y="80" font-size="7" fill="' + lc + '">15ft EQ</text>';
  } else if (type === '90_square') {
    // RETURN: 90deg square turn — WARNING
    s += '<rect x="5" y="25" width="40" height="50" rx="4" fill="' + bg + '" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<text x="25" y="54" text-anchor="middle" font-size="9" fill="#aaa">AHU</text>';
    s += '<rect x="45" y="20" width="55" height="60" rx="0" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<rect x="62" y="80" width="20" height="30" rx="0" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    // Sharp corner
    s += '<line x1="62" y1="80" x2="82" y2="80" stroke="#d32f2f" stroke-width="3"/>';
    // Turbulence
    s += '<circle cx="75" cy="65" r="3" stroke="#d32f2f" stroke-width="1" fill="none" opacity=".5"/>';
    s += '<circle cx="85" cy="72" r="2.5" stroke="#d32f2f" stroke-width="1" fill="none" opacity=".5"/>';
    // Airflow toward AHU
    s += '<line x1="72" y1="105" x2="72" y2="82" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<path d="M72 75 Q72 50 50 45" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="50,40 42,45 50,50" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    s += '<rect x="120" y="60" width="60" height="18" rx="4" fill="#d32f2f" opacity=".15" stroke="#d32f2f" stroke-width="1"/>';
    s += '<text x="150" y="72" text-anchor="middle" font-size="8" font-weight="bold" fill="#d32f2f">\u26A0 120ft EQ</text>';
  } else if (type === '90_vanes') {
    // RETURN: 90deg with vanes, air toward AHU
    s += '<rect x="5" y="25" width="40" height="50" rx="4" fill="' + bg + '" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<text x="25" y="54" text-anchor="middle" font-size="9" fill="#aaa">AHU</text>';
    s += '<rect x="45" y="20" width="50" height="60" rx="3" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<rect x="58" y="80" width="24" height="30" rx="3" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    // Turning vanes
    s += '<path d="M65 75 Q65 55 50 45" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<path d="M72 75 Q72 52 55 40" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<path d="M78 75 Q78 48 60 35" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>';
    // Airflow toward AHU
    s += '<line x1="70" y1="105" x2="70" y2="82" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<path d="M70 75 Q70 50 50 42" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="50,37 42,42 50,47" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    s += '<text x="130" y="60" font-size="7" fill="' + lc + '">20ft EQ</text>';
  } else if (type === 'platform_mac') {
    // RETURN: Dust Free Platform MAC — compact 90deg bottom return
    s += '<rect x="60" y="5" width="40" height="55" rx="4" fill="' + bg + '" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<text x="80" y="35" text-anchor="middle" font-size="8" fill="#aaa">AHU</text>';
    // MAC box (wide, short, sits under AHU)
    s += '<rect x="30" y="60" width="100" height="35" rx="4" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    // Filter inside MAC (diagonal pattern)
    s += '<line x1="55" y1="62" x2="55" y2="93" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="1" stroke-dasharray="3 2"/>';
    s += '<line x1="65" y1="62" x2="65" y2="93" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="1" stroke-dasharray="3 2"/>';
    s += '<line x1="75" y1="62" x2="75" y2="93" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="1" stroke-dasharray="3 2"/>';
    s += '<line x1="85" y1="62" x2="85" y2="93" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="1" stroke-dasharray="3 2"/>';
    s += '<line x1="95" y1="62" x2="95" y2="93" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="1" stroke-dasharray="3 2"/>';
    s += '<line x1="105" y1="62" x2="105" y2="93" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="1" stroke-dasharray="3 2"/>';
    // Return duct entering from side
    s += '<rect x="130" y="67" width="40" height="22" rx="3" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    // Air: from return duct into MAC
    s += '<line x1="165" y1="78" x2="133" y2="78" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="133,73 125,78 133,83" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    // Air: up through filter into AHU
    s += '<line x1="80" y1="60" x2="80" y2="40" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="76,40 80,32 84,40" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    // Labels
    s += '<text x="80" y="108" text-anchor="middle" font-size="7" fill="' + wc + '">Dust Free Platform MAC</text>';
    s += '<text x="80" y="116" text-anchor="middle" font-size="6" fill="' + lc + '">15ft EQ \u2014 Built-in MERV 11-13 filter</text>';
  } else {
    // Generic fallback
    s += '<rect x="5" y="30" width="40" height="60" rx="4" fill="' + bg + '" stroke="' + lc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<text x="25" y="64" text-anchor="middle" font-size="9" fill="#aaa">AHU</text>';
    s += '<rect x="45" y="35" width="80" height="50" rx="3" stroke="' + wc + '" stroke-width="2" fill="none"/>';
    s += '<line x1="55" y1="60" x2="115" y2="60" class="plenum-flow" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
  }
  s += '</svg>';
  return s;
}

function wizUpdatePlenumSVGs() {
  var supEl = document.getElementById('supPlenumSVG');
  var plTypeEl = document.getElementById('plType');
  if (supEl && plTypeEl) supEl.innerHTML = wizPlenumSVG(plTypeEl.value, false);
  var retEl = document.getElementById('retPlenumSVG');
  var retPlTypeEl = document.getElementById('retPlType');
  if (retEl && retPlTypeEl) retEl.innerHTML = wizPlenumSVG(retPlTypeEl.value, true);
}

// ---- Unit Configuration SVG ----
// Shows complete equipment + plenum layout based on equipType, airflowDir, returnPosition
function wizUnitConfigSVG() {
  var sc = '#d32f2f'; // supply color
  var rc = '#ff9800'; // return color
  var ac = '#4caf50'; // airflow arrows
  var bg = '#333';    // equipment box
  var lc = '#888';    // label color
  var dir = WIZ.airflowDir || 'upflow';
  var equip = WIZ.equipType || 'air_handler';
  var retPos = WIZ.returnPosition || 'bottom';
  var equipLabel = equip === 'gas_furnace' ? 'Gas Furnace' : 'Air Handler';
  var s = '';

  if (dir === 'upflow') {
    s += '<svg viewBox="0 0 240 200" width="100%" style="max-width:280px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">';
    // Supply plenum at top
    s += '<rect x="70" y="8" width="100" height="24" rx="3" fill="none" stroke="' + sc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<text x="120" y="23" text-anchor="middle" fill="' + lc + '" font-size="9">Supply Plenum</text>';
    // Supply collars exiting sides
    s += '<rect x="42" y="14" width="28" height="12" rx="6" fill="none" stroke="' + sc + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
    s += '<rect x="170" y="14" width="28" height="12" rx="6" fill="none" stroke="' + sc + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
    s += '<line x1="42" y1="20" x2="26" y2="20" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="26,17 20,20 26,23" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    s += '<line x1="198" y1="20" x2="214" y2="20" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="214,17 220,20 214,23" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    // Upward arrow from equipment to supply
    s += '<line x1="120" y1="60" x2="120" y2="36" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="116,38 120,30 124,38" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    // Equipment box
    s += '<rect x="60" y="60" width="120" height="60" rx="4" fill="' + bg + '"/>';
    s += '<text x="120" y="88" text-anchor="middle" fill="#fff" font-size="11" font-weight="bold">' + equipLabel + '</text>';
    s += '<text x="120" y="100" text-anchor="middle" fill="#aaa" font-size="8">▲ UPFLOW</text>';

    if (retPos === 'bottom' || equip === 'air_handler') {
      // Return plenum at bottom
      s += '<line x1="120" y1="120" x2="120" y2="146" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="116,142 120,150 124,142" fill="' + ac + '" transform="rotate(180 120 142)"/>';
      s += '<rect x="70" y="152" width="100" height="24" rx="3" fill="none" stroke="' + rc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
      s += '<text x="120" y="167" text-anchor="middle" fill="' + lc + '" font-size="9">Return Plenum</text>';
      // Return collars entering sides
      s += '<rect x="42" y="158" width="28" height="12" rx="6" fill="none" stroke="' + rc + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
      s += '<rect x="170" y="158" width="28" height="12" rx="6" fill="none" stroke="' + rc + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
      s += '<line x1="20" y1="164" x2="42" y2="164" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="38,161 44,164 38,167" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
      s += '<line x1="220" y1="164" x2="198" y2="164" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
      s += '<polygon points="202,161 196,164 202,167" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    } else {
      // Side return (gas furnace)
      var sideX = retPos === 'side_left' ? 60 : 180;
      var arrDir = retPos === 'side_left' ? -1 : 1;
      var startX = retPos === 'side_left' ? 26 : 214;
      var endX = sideX;
      s += '<line x1="' + startX + '" y1="90" x2="' + endX + '" y2="90" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
      if (retPos === 'side_left') {
        s += '<polygon points="' + (endX - 4) + ',87 ' + (endX + 2) + ',90 ' + (endX - 4) + ',93" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
      } else {
        s += '<polygon points="' + (endX + 4) + ',87 ' + (endX - 2) + ',90 ' + (endX + 4) + ',93" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
      }
      // Return duct label
      var lblX = retPos === 'side_left' ? 10 : 210;
      s += '<text x="' + lblX + '" y="82" text-anchor="' + (retPos === 'side_left' ? 'start' : 'end') + '" fill="' + rc + '" font-size="8">Return</text>';
      // "No bottom plenum" note
      s += '<text x="120" y="142" text-anchor="middle" fill="' + lc + '" font-size="8" font-style="italic">Side return — no bottom plenum</text>';
    }
    s += '</svg>';

  } else if (dir === 'downflow') {
    s += '<svg viewBox="0 0 240 200" width="100%" style="max-width:280px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">';
    // Return plenum at top (air enters from top in downflow)
    s += '<rect x="70" y="8" width="100" height="24" rx="3" fill="none" stroke="' + rc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<text x="120" y="23" text-anchor="middle" fill="' + lc + '" font-size="9">Return Plenum</text>';
    // Return collars entering sides
    s += '<rect x="42" y="14" width="28" height="12" rx="6" fill="none" stroke="' + rc + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
    s += '<rect x="170" y="14" width="28" height="12" rx="6" fill="none" stroke="' + rc + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
    s += '<line x1="20" y1="20" x2="42" y2="20" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="38,17 44,20 38,23" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    s += '<line x1="220" y1="20" x2="198" y2="20" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="202,17 196,20 202,23" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    // Downward arrow from return plenum into equipment
    s += '<line x1="120" y1="32" x2="120" y2="56" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="116,52 120,60 124,52" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    // Equipment box
    s += '<rect x="60" y="60" width="120" height="60" rx="4" fill="' + bg + '"/>';
    s += '<text x="120" y="88" text-anchor="middle" fill="#fff" font-size="11" font-weight="bold">' + equipLabel + '</text>';
    s += '<text x="120" y="100" text-anchor="middle" fill="#aaa" font-size="8">▼ DOWNFLOW</text>';
    // Downward arrow from equipment to supply
    s += '<line x1="120" y1="120" x2="120" y2="148" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="116,144 120,152 124,144" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    // Supply plenum at bottom
    s += '<rect x="70" y="152" width="100" height="24" rx="3" fill="none" stroke="' + sc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<text x="120" y="167" text-anchor="middle" fill="' + lc + '" font-size="9">Supply Plenum</text>';
    // Supply collars exiting sides
    s += '<rect x="42" y="158" width="28" height="12" rx="6" fill="none" stroke="' + sc + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
    s += '<rect x="170" y="158" width="28" height="12" rx="6" fill="none" stroke="' + sc + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
    s += '<line x1="42" y1="164" x2="26" y2="164" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="26,161 20,164 26,167" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    s += '<line x1="198" y1="164" x2="214" y2="164" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="214,161 220,164 214,167" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    s += '</svg>';

  } else if (dir === 'horizontal_left') {
    s += '<svg viewBox="0 0 280 160" width="100%" style="max-width:320px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">';
    // Return side (right) — air enters from right
    s += '<rect x="210" y="40" width="24" height="80" rx="3" fill="none" stroke="' + rc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<text x="222" y="135" text-anchor="middle" fill="' + lc + '" font-size="8">Return</text>';
    // Return collars top/bottom
    s += '<rect x="216" y="22" width="12" height="18" rx="6" fill="none" stroke="' + rc + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
    s += '<rect x="216" y="120" width="12" height="18" rx="6" fill="none" stroke="' + rc + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
    s += '<line x1="222" y1="10" x2="222" y2="22" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="219,22 222,28 225,22" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    s += '<line x1="222" y1="150" x2="222" y2="138" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="219,138 222,132 225,138" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    // Arrow: return plenum → equipment
    s += '<line x1="210" y1="80" x2="188" y2="80" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="192,77 186,80 192,83" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    // Equipment box
    s += '<rect x="80" y="40" width="108" height="80" rx="4" fill="' + bg + '"/>';
    s += '<text x="134" y="76" text-anchor="middle" fill="#fff" font-size="11" font-weight="bold">' + equipLabel + '</text>';
    s += '<text x="134" y="90" text-anchor="middle" fill="#aaa" font-size="8">◀ HORIZONTAL LEFT</text>';
    // Arrow: equipment → supply
    s += '<line x1="80" y1="80" x2="58" y2="80" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="62,77 56,80 62,83" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    // Supply side (left)
    s += '<rect x="34" y="40" width="24" height="80" rx="3" fill="none" stroke="' + sc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<text x="46" y="135" text-anchor="middle" fill="' + lc + '" font-size="8">Supply</text>';
    // Supply collars top/bottom
    s += '<rect x="40" y="22" width="12" height="18" rx="6" fill="none" stroke="' + sc + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
    s += '<rect x="40" y="120" width="12" height="18" rx="6" fill="none" stroke="' + sc + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
    s += '<line x1="46" y1="22" x2="46" y2="10" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="43,14 46,8 49,14" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    s += '<line x1="46" y1="138" x2="46" y2="150" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="43,146 46,152 49,146" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    s += '</svg>';

  } else if (dir === 'horizontal_right') {
    s += '<svg viewBox="0 0 280 160" width="100%" style="max-width:320px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">';
    // Return side (left) — air enters from left
    s += '<rect x="34" y="40" width="24" height="80" rx="3" fill="none" stroke="' + rc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<text x="46" y="135" text-anchor="middle" fill="' + lc + '" font-size="8">Return</text>';
    // Return collars top/bottom
    s += '<rect x="40" y="22" width="12" height="18" rx="6" fill="none" stroke="' + rc + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
    s += '<rect x="40" y="120" width="12" height="18" rx="6" fill="none" stroke="' + rc + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
    s += '<line x1="46" y1="10" x2="46" y2="22" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="43,22 46,28 49,22" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    s += '<line x1="46" y1="150" x2="46" y2="138" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="43,138 46,132 49,138" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    // Arrow: return plenum → equipment
    s += '<line x1="58" y1="80" x2="78" y2="80" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="74,77 80,80 74,83" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    // Equipment box
    s += '<rect x="80" y="40" width="108" height="80" rx="4" fill="' + bg + '"/>';
    s += '<text x="134" y="76" text-anchor="middle" fill="#fff" font-size="11" font-weight="bold">' + equipLabel + '</text>';
    s += '<text x="134" y="90" text-anchor="middle" fill="#aaa" font-size="8">HORIZONTAL RIGHT ▶</text>';
    // Arrow: equipment → supply
    s += '<line x1="188" y1="80" x2="208" y2="80" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="204,77 210,80 204,83" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    // Supply side (right)
    s += '<rect x="210" y="40" width="24" height="80" rx="3" fill="none" stroke="' + sc + '" stroke-width="2"/>';
    s += '<text x="222" y="135" text-anchor="middle" fill="' + lc + '" font-size="8">Supply</text>';
    // Supply collars top/bottom
    s += '<rect x="216" y="22" width="12" height="18" rx="6" fill="none" stroke="' + sc + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
    s += '<rect x="216" y="120" width="12" height="18" rx="6" fill="none" stroke="' + sc + '" stroke-width="1.5"/>';
    s += '<line x1="222" y1="22" x2="222" y2="10" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="219,14 222,8 225,14" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    s += '<line x1="222" y1="138" x2="222" y2="150" stroke="' + ac + '" stroke-width="2" class="plenum-flow"/>';
    s += '<polygon points="219,146 222,152 225,146" fill="' + ac + '"/>';
    s += '</svg>';
  }

  return s;
}

function wizUpdateUnitConfigSVG() {
  var el = document.getElementById('wizUnitConfigSVG');
  if (el) el.innerHTML = wizUnitConfigSVG();
}

// ---- navigation ----
function wizGoTo(step) {
  step = parseInt(step);
  if (step === WIZ.step) return;

  // Save any open branch form before leaving step 3
  if (WIZ.step === 3 && WIZ.activeBranch >= 0) {
    wizSaveBranch(WIZ.activeBranch);
    WIZ.activeBranch = -1;
  }
  // Save trunk fields before leaving step 2
  if (WIZ.step === 2) {
    wizSaveTrunks();
  }

  // Init downstream data
  if (step === 2 && WIZ.trunks.length === 0) wizInitTrunks();
  if (step === 3 && WIZ.branches.length === 0) wizInitBranches();
  if (step === 4) wizCalcResults();

  var prev = document.getElementById('wizStep' + WIZ.step);
  if (prev) prev.classList.remove('active');

  WIZ.step = step;

  var next = document.getElementById('wizStep' + step);
  if (next) next.classList.add('active');

  wizUpdateBar();

  if (step === 2) wizRenderTrunks();
  if (step === 3) wizRenderBranches();
  if (step === 4) wizRenderResults();

  // Scroll to wizard step bar
  var bar = document.getElementById('wizStepBar');
  if (bar) bar.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
}

function wizUpdateBar() {
  var pcts = ['8%','33%','66%','100%'];
  var fill = document.getElementById('wizProgressFill');
  if (fill) fill.style.width = pcts[WIZ.step - 1];

  [1,2,3,4].forEach(function(n) {
    var pill = document.getElementById('wizPill' + n);
    if (!pill) return;
    pill.classList.remove('active','done');
    if (n === WIZ.step) pill.classList.add('active');
    else if (n < WIZ.step) pill.classList.add('done');
  });
}

// ---- STEP 1 ----
// Layout / airPath / material are toggled directly by click handler

// ---- STEP 2: TRUNKS ----
// Recommend a round duct size for given CFM + material
// Uses Manual D velocity limits: supply trunk 900, supply branch 600, return trunk 700, return branch 600
function wizRecommendSize(cfm, isReturn, isTrunk, material, compression) {
  var maxVel = isTrunk ? (isReturn ? 700 : 900) : (material === 'flex' ? 700 : 900);
  var isFlex = material === 'flex';
  var comp = compression || 0;
  if (isFlex && comp === 0) comp = 10; // Default assumed compression for flex (realistic field minimum)

  var WIZ_REC_SIZES = [4,5,6,7,8,9,10,12,14,16,18,20,22,24];
  for (var si = 0; si < WIZ_REC_SIZES.length; si++) {
    var d = WIZ_REC_SIZES[si];
    var area = Math.PI * Math.pow(d / 12 / 2, 2);
    var vel = cfm / area;
    // Check velocity
    if (vel > maxVel) continue;
    // Check friction rate with compression/ductboard factor
    if (typeof frictionLoss === 'function') {
      var fr = frictionLoss(d, cfm);
      if (isFlex) fr *= wizFlexFactor(comp);
      else if (material === 'ductboard') fr *= 1.2;
      if (fr > 0.08) continue;
    }
    return String(d);
  }
  return '24';
}

function wizInitTrunks() {
  WIZ.trunks = [];
  var layout = WIZ.layout;

  // Auto-create from plenum collars if any exist
  var supplyCollars = (typeof SS !== 'undefined' && SS.collars) ? SS.collars : [];
  var returnCollars = (typeof SS !== 'undefined' && SS.retCollars) ? SS.retCollars : [];
  var hasCollars = supplyCollars.length > 0 || returnCollars.length > 0;

  if (hasCollars) {
    // Create supply trunks from supply collars
    supplyCollars.forEach(function(col, i) {
      WIZ.trunks.push({
        label: 'Supply ' + (i + 1) + ' (' + col.size + '\u2033)',
        airPath: 'supply', isRadial: false, shape: 'round',
        size: col.size, width: col.size, height: '8',
        length: '20', elbows90: 0, elbows45: 0
      });
    });
    // Create return trunks from return collars
    returnCollars.forEach(function(col, i) {
      WIZ.trunks.push({
        label: 'Return ' + (i + 1) + ' (' + col.size + '\u2033)',
        airPath: 'return', isRadial: false, shape: 'round',
        size: col.size, width: col.size, height: '8',
        length: '15', elbows90: 0, elbows45: 0
      });
    });
    if (WIZ.trunks.length > 0) return;
  }

  // Fallback: layout-based defaults
  if (layout === 'RADIAL') {
    WIZ.trunks.push({ label:'Plenum', airPath:'supply', isRadial:true, shape:'round', size:'12', width:'12', height:'10', length:'0', elbows90:0, elbows45:0, material:'metal', compression:0 });
    return;
  }
  if (layout === 'LR') {
    WIZ.trunks.push({ label:'Left Trunk',  airPath:'supply', isRadial:false, shape:'round', size:'12', width:'12', height:'10', length:'20', elbows90:0, elbows45:0, material:'metal', compression:0 });
    WIZ.trunks.push({ label:'Right Trunk', airPath:'supply', isRadial:false, shape:'round', size:'12', width:'12', height:'10', length:'20', elbows90:0, elbows45:0, material:'metal', compression:0 });
    return;
  }
  if (layout === '1SIDE') {
    WIZ.trunks.push({ label:'Main Trunk', airPath:'supply', isRadial:false, shape:'round', size:'12', width:'12', height:'10', length:'30', elbows90:0, elbows45:0, material:'metal', compression:0 });
    return;
  }
  WIZ.trunks.push({ label:'Trunk A', airPath:'supply', isRadial:false, shape:'round', size:'12', width:'12', height:'10', length:'20', elbows90:0, elbows45:0, material:'metal', compression:0 });
}

function wizRenderTrunks() {
  var html = '';
  WIZ.trunks.forEach(function(t, i) {
    html += '<div class="wiz-trunk-card" id="wizTrunkCard' + i + '">';
    html += '<div class="wiz-trunk-label-row">';
    html += '<div class="wiz-trunk-label">' + wizSvg('trunk') + '<span>' + t.label + '</span></div>';
    if (!t.isRadial || WIZ.trunks.length > 1) {
      html += '<div class="wiz-trunk-remove" data-wiz-trunk-rm="' + i + '">' + wizSvg('remove') + '</div>';
    }
    html += '</div>';

    if (!t.isRadial) {
      // Air path toggle (Supply / Return)
      var ap = t.airPath || 'supply';
      html += '<div class="wiz-shape-toggle" style="margin-bottom:8px">';
      html += '<div class="wiz-shape-btn' + (ap === 'supply' ? ' active' : '') + '" data-wiz-trunk-ap="' + i + '" data-ap="supply" style="' + (ap === 'supply' ? 'background:#d32f2f;border-color:#d32f2f' : '') + '">';
      html += '<svg width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M12 19V5M5 12l7-7 7 7"/></svg> Supply</div>';
      html += '<div class="wiz-shape-btn' + (ap === 'return' ? ' active' : '') + '" data-wiz-trunk-ap="' + i + '" data-ap="return" style="' + (ap === 'return' ? 'background:#ff9800;border-color:#ff9800' : '') + '">';
      html += '<svg width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M12 5v14M5 12l7 7 7-7"/></svg> Return</div>';
      html += '</div>';

      // Material toggle (Metal / Flex / Ductboard)
      var tMat = t.material || 'metal';
      html += '<div class="wiz-shape-toggle" style="margin-bottom:8px">';
      html += '<div class="wiz-shape-btn' + (tMat === 'metal' ? ' active' : '') + '" data-wiz-trunk-mat="' + i + '" data-tmatval="metal">' + wizSvg('rect') + ' Metal</div>';
      html += '<div class="wiz-shape-btn' + (tMat === 'flex' ? ' active' : '') + '" data-wiz-trunk-mat="' + i + '" data-tmatval="flex">' + wizSvg('round') + ' Flex</div>';
      html += '<div class="wiz-shape-btn' + (tMat === 'ductboard' ? ' active' : '') + '" data-wiz-trunk-mat="' + i + '" data-tmatval="ductboard">' + wizSvg('rect') + ' Ductboard</div>';
      html += '</div>';

      // Trunk compression (flex only)
      if (tMat === 'flex') {
        var tComp = t.compression || 0;
        var tFF = tComp ? wizFlexFactor(tComp) : 1;
        var tFFText = tComp ? 'Friction \u00D7' + tFF.toFixed(2) : '<span style="color:#d32f2f">Set trunk compression</span>';
        html += '<div style="background:#1a1a1a;border:1px solid ' + (tComp ? '#444' : '#d32f2f') + ';border-radius:8px;padding:8px;margin-bottom:8px">';
        html += '<div class="wiz-input-label" style="margin-bottom:4px">Trunk Compression</div>';
        html += '<div style="display:flex;gap:3px;flex-wrap:wrap;margin-bottom:6px">';
        WIZ_COMPRESS.forEach(function(c){
          var isA = tComp == c;
          html += '<div class="compression-preset-btn' + (isA ? ' active' : '') + '" data-wiz-trunk-comp-preset="' + i + '" data-wiz-tcomp-val="' + c + '" style="cursor:pointer;padding:4px 8px;border-radius:5px;font-size:11px;font-weight:600;border:1px solid ' + (isA ? '#d32f2f' : '#555') + ';background:' + (isA ? '#d32f2f' : '#2a2a2a') + ';color:' + (isA ? '#fff' : '#ccc') + '">' + c + '%</div>';
        });
        html += '</div>';
        html += '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px">';
        html += '<input type="range" style="flex:1" min="4" max="30" step="1" value="' + (tComp || 4) + '" data-wiz-trunk-compress="' + i + '">';
        html += '<input type="number" class="slider-value-input" style="width:48px;text-align:center" min="4" max="30" step="1" value="' + (tComp || '') + '" placeholder="%" data-wiz-trunk-comp-input="' + i + '">';
        html += '<span style="font-size:10px;color:#888">%</span>';
        html += '</div>';
        html += '<div style="font-size:11px;margin-top:4px;color:' + (tComp ? '#ff9800' : '#d32f2f') + '">' + tFFText + '</div>';
        html += '</div>';
      }

      // Ductboard properties (always rectangular, built-in R-value)
      if (tMat === 'ductboard') {
        t.compression = 0; // no compression for rigid ductboard
        html += '<div style="background:#1a1a1a;border:1px solid #444;border-radius:8px;padding:8px;margin-bottom:8px">';
        html += '<div class="wiz-input-label" style="margin-bottom:4px">Ductboard R-Value (built-in insulation)</div>';
        html += '<select class="input-field" data-wiz-trunk-dbr="' + i + '" style="width:100%">';
        var dbR = t.ductboardR || 'R6';
        html += '<option value="R4.2"' + (dbR === 'R4.2' ? ' selected' : '') + '>R-4.2 (1\u2033 board)</option>';
        html += '<option value="R6"' + (dbR === 'R6' ? ' selected' : '') + '>R-6 (1.5\u2033 board) \u2014 code minimum</option>';
        html += '<option value="R8"' + (dbR === 'R8' ? ' selected' : '') + '>R-8 (2\u2033 board)</option>';
        html += '</select>';
        html += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:#888;margin-top:4px">Ductboard: rigid fiberglass panels. 1.2\u00D7 friction vs metal. No separate insulation needed.</div>';
        html += '</div>';
      }

      // Shape toggle (no Rect option for flex — flex is always round; ductboard is always rect)
      if (tMat === 'flex') {
        t.shape = 'round'; // force round for flex
        html += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:#888;margin-bottom:6px;font-style:italic">Flex duct is always round</div>';
      } else if (tMat === 'ductboard') {
        t.shape = 'rect'; // ductboard is always rectangular
        html += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:#888;margin-bottom:6px;font-style:italic">Ductboard is always rectangular (flat panels)</div>';
      } else {
        html += '<div class="wiz-shape-toggle">';
        html += '<div class="wiz-shape-btn' + (t.shape !== 'rect' ? ' active' : '') + '" data-wiz-trunk-shape="' + i + '" data-shape="round">' + wizSvg('round') + ' Round</div>';
        html += '<div class="wiz-shape-btn' + (t.shape === 'rect' ? ' active' : '') + '" data-wiz-trunk-shape="' + i + '" data-shape="rect">' + wizSvg('rect') + ' Rect</div>';
        html += '</div>';
      }

      // Size
      if (t.shape === 'rect') {
        html += '<div class="wiz-input-row">';
        html += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Width (in)</div>';
        html += '<select class="input-field" data-wiz-trunk-w="' + i + '">';
        WIZ_RECT_DIMS.forEach(function(v){ html += '<option value="' + v + '"' + (t.width == v ? ' selected':'') + '>' + v + '"</option>'; });
        html += '</select></div>';
        html += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Height (in)</div>';
        html += '<select class="input-field" data-wiz-trunk-h="' + i + '">';
        WIZ_RECT_DIMS.forEach(function(v){ html += '<option value="' + v + '"' + (t.height == v ? ' selected':'') + '>' + v + '"</option>'; });
        html += '</select></div>';
        html += '</div>';
        var deq = wizRectEqDia(t.width, t.height);
        html += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:#888;margin-bottom:8px">Equiv. dia: <span style="color:#ff9800;font-family:\'SF Mono\',monospace">' + deq.toFixed(1) + '"</span></div>';
      } else {
        html += '<div class="wiz-input-row">';
        html += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Size</div>';
        html += '<select class="input-field" data-wiz-trunk-size="' + i + '">';
        WIZ_ROUND_SIZES.forEach(function(v){ html += '<option value="' + v + '"' + (t.size == v ? ' selected':'') + '>' + v + '\u2033</option>'; });
        html += '</select></div>';
        html += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Length (ft)</div>';
        html += '<input type="number" class="input-field" value="' + (t.length || '') + '" min="0" max="500" data-wiz-trunk-len="' + i + '"></div>';
        html += '</div>';
      }
      if (t.shape === 'rect') {
        html += '<div class="wiz-input-row">';
        html += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Length (ft)</div>';
        html += '<input type="number" class="input-field" value="' + (t.length || '') + '" min="0" max="500" data-wiz-trunk-len="' + i + '"></div>';
        html += '<div class="wiz-input-group"></div>';
        html += '</div>';
      }

      // Elbows
      html += '<div class="wiz-input-row">';
      html += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">90\u00B0 Elbows</div>';
      html += '<input type="number" class="input-field" value="' + (t.elbows90 || 0) + '" min="0" max="20" data-wiz-trunk-e90="' + i + '"></div>';
      html += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">45\u00B0 Elbows</div>';
      html += '<input type="number" class="input-field" value="' + (t.elbows45 || 0) + '" min="0" max="20" data-wiz-trunk-e45="' + i + '"></div>';
      html += '</div>';

      // Label
      html += '<div class="wiz-input-row">';
      html += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Label</div>';
      html += '<input type="text" class="input-field" value="' + t.label + '" data-wiz-trunk-lbl="' + i + '"></div>';
      html += '</div>';
    }
    html += '</div>'; // /trunk-card
  });

  var el = document.getElementById('wizTrunkCards');
  if (el) el.innerHTML = html;
}

function wizSaveTrunks() {
  WIZ.trunks.forEach(function(t, i) {
    var lbl = document.querySelector('[data-wiz-trunk-lbl="' + i + '"]');
    var size = document.querySelector('[data-wiz-trunk-size="' + i + '"]');
    var len = document.querySelector('[data-wiz-trunk-len="' + i + '"]');
    var e90 = document.querySelector('[data-wiz-trunk-e90="' + i + '"]');
    var e45 = document.querySelector('[data-wiz-trunk-e45="' + i + '"]');
    var w = document.querySelector('[data-wiz-trunk-w="' + i + '"]');
    var h = document.querySelector('[data-wiz-trunk-h="' + i + '"]');
    if (lbl) t.label = lbl.value;
    if (size) t.size = size.value;
    if (len) t.length = len.value;
    if (e90) t.elbows90 = parseInt(e90.value) || 0;
    if (e45) t.elbows45 = parseInt(e45.value) || 0;
    if (w) t.width = w.value;
    if (h) t.height = h.value;
    var dbr = document.querySelector('[data-wiz-trunk-dbr="' + i + '"]');
    if (dbr) t.ductboardR = dbr.value;
  });
  if (typeof wizAutoSave === 'function') wizAutoSave();
}

// ---- STEP 3: BRANCHES ----
function wizInitBranches() {
  if (WIZ.branches.length > 0) return;

  // Get rooms from Rooms tab
  var rooms = getRoomsList(); // [{name, cfm}, ...]
  var supplyTrunks = WIZ.trunks.filter(function(t){ return t.airPath === 'supply'; });
  var returnTrunks = WIZ.trunks.filter(function(t){ return t.airPath === 'return'; });

  var num = 1;

  if (rooms.length > 0 && supplyTrunks.length > 0) {
    // Distribute rooms evenly across supply trunks
    var perTrunk = Math.ceil(rooms.length / supplyTrunks.length);
    var ri = 0;
    supplyTrunks.forEach(function(trunk) {
      var ti = WIZ.trunks.indexOf(trunk);
      for (var b = 0; b < perTrunk && ri < rooms.length; b++, ri++) {
        var rm = rooms[ri];
        var isReturn = false;
        var recSize = rm.cfm ? wizRecommendSize(rm.cfm, isReturn, false, WIZ.material, 8) : '6';
        WIZ.branches.push({
          trunkIdx: ti, num: num, room: rm.name,
          cfm: rm.cfm || '', shape: 'round',
          size: recSize, width: '8', height: '8',
          material: WIZ.material, compression: WIZ.material === 'flex' ? 10 : 0,
          length: '12', fittings: [], bootType: '90boot', takeoffType: 'straight90',
          done: false, recommended: recSize
        });
        num++;
      }
    });

    // Add one return branch per return trunk (whole-house return)
    returnTrunks.forEach(function(trunk) {
      var ti = WIZ.trunks.indexOf(trunk);
      var totalCfm = getRoomsTotalCFM();
      var retCfm = returnTrunks.length > 0 ? Math.round(totalCfm / returnTrunks.length) : totalCfm;
      var recSize = retCfm ? wizRecommendSize(retCfm, true, false, WIZ.material, 10) : '14';
      WIZ.branches.push({
        trunkIdx: ti, num: num, room: 'Return ' + (num - rooms.length),
        cfm: retCfm || '', shape: 'round',
        size: recSize, width: '14', height: '10',
        material: WIZ.material, compression: WIZ.material === 'flex' ? 10 : 0,
        length: '10', fittings: [], bootType: 'wallReg', takeoffType: 'straight90',
        done: false, recommended: recSize
      });
      num++;
    });
  } else {
    // Fallback: generic branches if no rooms data
    var total = WIZ.layout === 'LR' ? 6 : (WIZ.layout === 'RADIAL' ? 6 : 4);
    WIZ.trunks.forEach(function(trunk, ti) {
      var count = Math.ceil(total / WIZ.trunks.length);
      for (var b = 0; b < count; b++) {
        WIZ.branches.push({
          trunkIdx: ti, num: num, room: 'Room ' + num,
          cfm: '', shape: 'round', size: '6',
          width: '8', height: '8', material: WIZ.material,
          compression: 0, length: '12', fittings: [],
          bootType: '90boot', takeoffType: 'straight90', done: false
        });
        num++;
      }
    });
  }
}

// Calculate max CFM a duct can carry at 0.08 IWC/100ft given size, material, compression
function wizMaxCFM(sizeInch, material, compression) {
  if (!sizeInch || sizeInch <= 0) return 0;
  var D = parseFloat(sizeInch);
  var A = Math.PI * Math.pow(D / 24, 2); // sq ft
  var isFlex = material === 'flex';
  var isDuctboard = material === 'ductboard';
  var ff = isDuctboard ? 1.2 : (isFlex ? wizFlexFactor(compression || 0) : 1);
  // Binary search for max CFM where friction * ff <= 0.08
  var lo = 0, hi = 900 * A; // velocity-capped
  var best = 0;
  for (var it = 0; it < 40; it++) {
    var mid = (lo + hi) / 2;
    var fr = frictionLoss(D, mid) * ff;
    if (fr <= 0.08) { best = mid; lo = mid; }
    else { hi = mid; }
    if (hi - lo < 0.5) break;
  }
  // Also cap by Manual D velocity (700 for flex, 900 for metal/ductboard supply, 700 for return)
  var maxVel = isFlex ? 700 : 900;
  var maxCFMvel = maxVel * A;
  if (best > maxCFMvel) best = maxCFMvel;
  return Math.round(best);
}

function wizRenderBranches() {
  var html = '';
  var lastTrunk = -1;

  WIZ.branches.forEach(function(br, i) {
    if (br.trunkIdx !== lastTrunk) {
      if (lastTrunk >= 0) html += '</div>'; // close prev trunk group branches
      var trunk = WIZ.trunks[br.trunkIdx];
      var tLabel = trunk ? trunk.label : 'Trunk';
      var tSize = trunk ? wizSizeLabel(trunk) : '';
      // Calculate trunk capacity and total CFM it needs to carry
      var trunkTotalCFM = 0;
      WIZ.branches.forEach(function(b) { if (b.trunkIdx === br.trunkIdx && b.cfm) trunkTotalCFM += parseFloat(b.cfm) || 0; });
      var trunkMaxCFM = trunk ? wizMaxCFM(trunk.size || wizEffDia(trunk), trunk.material, trunk.compression) : 0;
      var trunkCfmOk = trunkMaxCFM >= trunkTotalCFM || trunkTotalCFM === 0;
      var trunkCfmTag = trunkTotalCFM > 0 ? '<span style="font-size:10px;margin-left:4px;color:' + (trunkCfmOk ? '#4caf50' : '#d32f2f') + ';font-weight:600">' + trunkTotalCFM + (trunkCfmOk ? '' : '/' + trunkMaxCFM + ' max') + ' CFM</span>' : '';

      html += '<div class="wiz-trunk-group">';
      html += '<div class="wiz-trunk-group-hdr">' + wizSvg('trunk');
      var apTag = trunk && trunk.airPath === 'return' ? '<span style="color:#ff9800;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;margin-left:6px;padding:1px 5px;border:1px solid #ff9800;border-radius:3px">RTN</span>' : '<span style="color:#d32f2f;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;margin-left:6px;padding:1px 5px;border:1px solid #d32f2f;border-radius:3px">SUP</span>';
      html += '<span class="wiz-trunk-group-lbl">\u21B3 Off ' + tLabel + (tSize && !trunk.isRadial ? ' (' + tSize + ')' : '') + apTag + trunkCfmTag + '</span></div>';
      html += '<div class="wiz-trunk-branches" data-wiz-trunk-branches="' + br.trunkIdx + '">';
      lastTrunk = br.trunkIdx;
    }

    var statusClass = br.done ? 'done' : (WIZ.activeBranch === i ? 'editing' : 'pending');
    var statusText  = br.done ? 'Done'  : (WIZ.activeBranch === i ? 'Editing' : 'Tap to edit');
    var shapeL = br.shape === 'rect' ? br.width + '\u00D7' + br.height + '"' : br.size + '\u2033';
    var matL   = br.material === 'flex' ? ' flex' : '';
    var fitL   = br.fittings.length ? ' \u00B7 ' + br.fittings.length + ' fit' : '';
    // Calculate actual capacity of this duct
    var brMaxCFM = wizMaxCFM(br.size, br.material, br.compression);
    var cfmL = '';
    if (br.cfm) {
      var cfmOk = brMaxCFM >= br.cfm;
      cfmL = ' \u00B7 <span style="color:' + (cfmOk ? '#4caf50' : '#d32f2f') + ';font-weight:600">' + br.cfm + (cfmOk ? '' : '/' + brMaxCFM + ' max') + ' CFM</span>';
    }

    html += '<div class="wiz-branch-item' + (WIZ.activeBranch === i ? ' editing' : '') + '" data-wiz-branch="' + i + '">';
    html += '<div class="wiz-branch-num">' + br.num + '</div>';
    html += '<div class="wiz-branch-info">';
    html += '<div class="wiz-branch-name">' + br.room + '</div>';
    var recL = br.recommended && br.size === br.recommended ? ' <span style="color:#4caf50">\u2713 rec</span>' : (br.recommended ? ' <span style="color:#ff9800">rec:' + br.recommended + '\u2033</span>' : '');
    html += '<div class="wiz-branch-detail">' + shapeL + matL + ' \u00B7 ' + br.length + ' ft' + fitL + cfmL + recL + '</div>';
    html += '</div>';
    html += '<div class="wiz-branch-badge ' + statusClass + '">' + statusText + '</div>';
    html += '</div>'; // /branch-item

    // Inline edit form
    if (WIZ.activeBranch === i) {
      html += wizRenderBranchForm(br, i);
    }
  });

  if (lastTrunk >= 0) html += '</div></div>'; // close last trunk group

  // Per-trunk "Add Branch" buttons
  if (WIZ.trunks.length > 0) {
    WIZ.trunks.forEach(function(trunk, ti) {
      var hasBranches = WIZ.branches.some(function(b){ return b.trunkIdx === ti; });
      if (!hasBranches) {
        html += '<div class="wiz-trunk-group">';
        html += '<div class="wiz-trunk-group-hdr">' + wizSvg('trunk');
        html += '<span class="wiz-trunk-group-lbl">\u21B3 Off ' + trunk.label + (trunk.isRadial ? '' : ' (' + wizSizeLabel(trunk) + ')') + '</span></div>';
        html += '<button class="wiz-add-branch-btn" data-wiz-add-branch="' + ti + '">' + wizSvg('branch') + 'Add Branch</button>';
        html += '</div>';
      }
    });
  }

  // Add-Branch buttons at bottom of each trunk's group
  // (Re-render adds them inline below each group)
  var el = document.getElementById('wizBranchArea');
  if (el) {
    el.innerHTML = html;

    // Append add-branch buttons under each trunk block
    WIZ.trunks.forEach(function(trunk, ti) {
      var groupEls = el.querySelectorAll('[data-wiz-trunk-branches="' + ti + '"]');
      groupEls.forEach(function(g) {
        var addBtn = document.createElement('button');
        addBtn.className = 'wiz-add-branch-btn';
        addBtn.setAttribute('data-wiz-add-branch', ti);
        addBtn.innerHTML = wizSvg('branch') + ' Add Branch to ' + trunk.label;
        g.parentNode.appendChild(addBtn);
      });
    });
  }
}

function wizRenderBranchForm(br, i) {
  var h = '';
  h += '<div class="wiz-branch-form">';

  // Room name + CFM
  h += '<div class="wiz-input-row">';
  h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Room Name</div>';
  h += '<input type="text" class="input-field" value="' + br.room + '" data-wiz-br-room="' + i + '"></div>';
  h += '<div class="wiz-input-group" style="max-width:90px"><div class="wiz-input-label">CFM</div>';
  h += '<input type="number" class="input-field" value="' + (br.cfm || '') + '" placeholder="CFM" min="0" max="9999" data-wiz-br-cfm="' + i + '"></div>';
  h += '</div>';

  // Material
  h += '<div class="wiz-input-label" style="margin-bottom:4px">Material</div>';
  h += '<div class="wiz-shape-toggle" style="margin-bottom:8px">';
  h += '<div class="wiz-shape-btn' + (br.material !== 'flex' ? ' active' : '') + '" data-wiz-br-mat="' + i + '" data-matval="metal">' + wizSvg('rect') + ' Metal</div>';
  h += '<div class="wiz-shape-btn' + (br.material === 'flex' ? ' active' : '') + '" data-wiz-br-mat="' + i + '" data-matval="flex">' + wizSvg('round') + ' Flex</div>';
  h += '</div>';

  // Compression (flex only) — user MUST set this, no assumptions
  if (br.material === 'flex') {
    var compVal = br.compression || '';
    var ff = compVal ? wizFlexFactor(compVal) : 1;
    var ffText = compVal ? 'Friction \u00D7' + ff.toFixed(2) : '<span style="color:#d32f2f">Set compression \u2014 measure the installed flex</span>';
    h += '<div class="wiz-compression-box" style="background:#1a1a1a;border:1px solid ' + (compVal ? '#444' : '#d32f2f') + ';border-radius:8px;padding:10px;margin:8px 0">';
    h += '<div class="wiz-input-label" style="margin-bottom:6px">Flex Compression Ratio</div>';
    h += '<div style="display:flex;gap:4px;flex-wrap:wrap;margin-bottom:8px">';
    WIZ_COMPRESS.forEach(function(c){
      var isActive = compVal == c;
      h += '<div class="compression-preset-btn' + (isActive ? ' active' : '') + '" data-wiz-comp-preset="' + i + '" data-wiz-comp-val="' + c + '" style="cursor:pointer;padding:6px 10px;border-radius:6px;font-size:12px;font-weight:600;border:1px solid ' + (isActive ? '#d32f2f' : '#555') + ';background:' + (isActive ? '#d32f2f' : '#2a2a2a') + ';color:' + (isActive ? '#fff' : '#ccc') + '">' + c + '%</div>';
    });
    h += '</div>';
    h += '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px">';
    h += '<input type="range" style="flex:1" min="4" max="30" step="1" value="' + (compVal || 4) + '" data-wiz-br-compress="' + i + '">';
    h += '<input type="number" class="slider-value-input" style="width:52px;text-align:center" min="4" max="30" step="1" value="' + (compVal || '') + '" placeholder="%" data-wiz-br-comp-input="' + i + '">';
    h += '<span style="font-size:11px;color:#888">%</span>';
    h += '</div>';
    h += '<div class="wiz-compression-val" style="margin-top:6px">' + ffText + '</div>';
    // Visual compression guide
    h += '<div style="margin-top:8px;padding:8px;background:#222;border-radius:6px;border:1px solid #333">';
    h += '<div style="font-size:10px;font-weight:600;color:#ff9800;margin-bottom:6px">Visual Guide — What does it look like?</div>';
    h += '<div style="display:flex;gap:6px;align-items:flex-end">';
    // 4% - stretched tight
    h += '<div style="flex:1;text-align:center"><svg viewBox="0 0 40 60" style="width:100%;max-width:40px"><rect x="5" y="2" width="30" height="56" rx="4" fill="none" stroke="#666" stroke-width="1"/>';
    for(var gi=0;gi<10;gi++) h += '<line x1="8" y1="'+(6+gi*5.4)+'" x2="32" y2="'+(6+gi*5.4)+'" stroke="#555" stroke-width="0.5"/>';
    h += '</svg><div style="font-size:9px;color:#4caf50;font-weight:600">4%</div><div style="font-size:8px;color:#888">Tight</div></div>';
    // 10%
    h += '<div style="flex:1;text-align:center"><svg viewBox="0 0 40 60" style="width:100%;max-width:40px"><rect x="5" y="2" width="30" height="56" rx="4" fill="none" stroke="#666" stroke-width="1"/>';
    for(var gi2=0;gi2<14;gi2++) h += '<line x1="8" y1="'+(5+gi2*3.8)+'" x2="32" y2="'+(5+gi2*3.8)+'" stroke="#888" stroke-width="0.7"/>';
    h += '</svg><div style="font-size:9px;color:#ff9800;font-weight:600">10%</div><div style="font-size:8px;color:#888">Visible</div></div>';
    // 20%
    h += '<div style="flex:1;text-align:center"><svg viewBox="0 0 40 60" style="width:100%;max-width:40px"><rect x="5" y="2" width="30" height="56" rx="4" fill="none" stroke="#666" stroke-width="1"/>';
    for(var gi3=0;gi3<22;gi3++) h += '<line x1="7" y1="'+(4+gi3*2.4)+'" x2="33" y2="'+(4+gi3*2.4)+'" stroke="#aaa" stroke-width="1"/>';
    h += '</svg><div style="font-size:9px;color:#d32f2f;font-weight:600">20%</div><div style="font-size:8px;color:#888">Bunched</div></div>';
    // 30%
    h += '<div style="flex:1;text-align:center"><svg viewBox="0 0 40 60" style="width:100%;max-width:40px"><rect x="5" y="2" width="30" height="56" rx="4" fill="none" stroke="#666" stroke-width="1"/>';
    for(var gi4=0;gi4<30;gi4++) h += '<line x1="6" y1="'+(3+gi4*1.8)+'" x2="34" y2="'+(3+gi4*1.8)+'" stroke="#ccc" stroke-width="1.2"/>';
    h += '</svg><div style="font-size:9px;color:#d32f2f;font-weight:600">30%</div><div style="font-size:8px;color:#888">Slinky</div></div>';
    h += '</div>';
    h += '<div style="font-size:9px;color:#888;margin-top:4px">Count wire spirals per foot: more spirals = more compression. If spirals are spread 3-4\u2033 apart = ~4%. Bunched tight <1\u2033 apart = 25%+.</div>';
    h += '</div>';
    h += '</div>';
  }

  // Shape (no Rect for flex — flex is always round)
  if (br.material === 'flex') {
    br.shape = 'round';
    h += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:#888;margin-bottom:6px;font-style:italic">Flex duct is always round</div>';
  } else {
    h += '<div class="wiz-input-label" style="margin-bottom:4px">Duct Shape</div>';
    h += '<div class="wiz-shape-toggle">';
    h += '<div class="wiz-shape-btn' + (br.shape !== 'rect' ? ' active' : '') + '" data-wiz-br-shape="' + i + '" data-shape="round">' + wizSvg('round') + ' Round</div>';
    h += '<div class="wiz-shape-btn' + (br.shape === 'rect' ? ' active' : '') + '" data-wiz-br-shape="' + i + '" data-shape="rect">' + wizSvg('rect') + ' Rect</div>';
    h += '</div>';
  }

  // Size fields
  if (br.shape === 'rect') {
    h += '<div class="wiz-input-row">';
    h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Width (in)</div>';
    h += '<select class="input-field" data-wiz-br-width="' + i + '">';
    WIZ_RECT_DIMS.forEach(function(v){ h += '<option value="' + v + '"' + (br.width == v ? ' selected':'') + '>' + v + '"</option>'; });
    h += '</select></div>';
    h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Height (in)</div>';
    h += '<select class="input-field" data-wiz-br-height="' + i + '">';
    WIZ_RECT_DIMS.forEach(function(v){ h += '<option value="' + v + '"' + (br.height == v ? ' selected':'') + '>' + v + '"</option>'; });
    h += '</select></div>';
    h += '</div>';
    var deq = wizRectEqDia(parseFloat(br.width) || 8, parseFloat(br.height) || 8);
    h += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:#888;margin-bottom:8px">Equiv. dia: <span style="color:#ff9800;font-family:\'SF Mono\',monospace">' + deq.toFixed(1) + '"</span></div>';
    h += '<div class="wiz-input-row">';
    h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Length (ft)</div>';
    h += '<input type="number" class="input-field" value="' + br.length + '" min="1" max="200" data-wiz-br-len="' + i + '"></div>';
    h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"></div>';
    h += '</div>';
  } else {
    h += '<div class="wiz-input-row">';
    h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Size</div>';
    h += '<select class="input-field" data-wiz-br-size="' + i + '">';
    [4,5,6,7,8,9,10,12,14,16].forEach(function(v){ h += '<option value="' + v + '"' + (br.size == v ? ' selected':'') + '>' + v + '\u2033</option>'; });
    h += '</select></div>';
    h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Length (ft)</div>';
    h += '<input type="number" class="input-field" value="' + br.length + '" min="1" max="200" data-wiz-br-len="' + i + '"></div>';
    h += '</div>';
  }

  // Takeoff type (how this branch connects to the trunk)
  h += '<div class="wiz-input-row">';
  h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Takeoff from Trunk</div>';
  h += '<select class="input-field" data-wiz-br-takeoff="' + i + '">';
  Object.keys(WIZ_TAKEOFF_TYPES).forEach(function(k){
    var to = WIZ_TAKEOFF_TYPES[k];
    h += '<option value="' + k + '"' + (br.takeoffType === k ? ' selected':'') + '>' + to.name + ' (' + to.eq + 'ft)</option>';
  });
  h += '</select></div>';
  h += '</div>';
  if (br.takeoffType && WIZ_TAKEOFF_TYPES[br.takeoffType]) {
    h += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:#888;margin-bottom:6px;margin-top:-4px">' + WIZ_TAKEOFF_TYPES[br.takeoffType].note + '</div>';
  }
  // Takeoff SVG illustration
  var takeoffSvg = wizTakeoffSVG(br.takeoffType || 'straight90');
  if (takeoffSvg) {
    h += '<div class="wiz-fitting-svg" data-svg-key="takeoff-' + (br.takeoffType || 'straight90') + '">' + takeoffSvg + '</div>';
  }

  // Boot type (what's at the end of the branch)
  h += '<div class="wiz-input-row">';
  h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Ends At (Register/Boot)</div>';
  h += '<select class="input-field" data-wiz-br-boot="' + i + '">';
  Object.keys(WIZ_BOOT_EQ).forEach(function(k){
    h += '<option value="' + k + '"' + (br.bootType === k ? ' selected':'') + '>' + WIZ_BOOT_EQ[k].name + '</option>';
  });
  h += '</select></div>';
  h += '</div>';
  // Boot SVG illustration
  var bootKey = br.bootType || 'straightboot';
  var bootPos = WIZ.bootPosition || 'floor';
  var bootSvgType = bootKey;
  if (bootKey === '90boot') bootSvgType = '90boot';
  else if (bootKey === 'straightboot') bootSvgType = 'straightboot';
  else if (bootKey === 'ceilTop' || bootKey === 'ceilSide') bootSvgType = 'register';
  else if (bootKey === 'floorReg') { bootSvgType = 'straightboot'; bootPos = 'floor'; }
  else if (bootKey === 'wallReg') bootSvgType = '90boot';
  var bootSvg = wizBootSVG(bootSvgType, bootPos);
  if (bootSvg) {
    h += '<div class="wiz-fitting-svg" data-svg-key="boot-' + bootKey + '">' + bootSvg + '</div>';
  }

  // Filter grill option (return branches only)
  var brTrunk = WIZ.trunks[br.trunkIdx];
  var isReturnBranch = brTrunk && brTrunk.airPath === 'return';
  if (isReturnBranch) {
    h += '<div style="margin-top:8px">';
    h += '<label class="input-label" style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;cursor:pointer">';
    h += '<input type="checkbox" data-wiz-br-filtergrill="' + i + '"' + (br.hasFilterGrill ? ' checked' : '') + '> Filter Grill (filter at register)';
    h += '</label>';
    h += '</div>';
    if (br.hasFilterGrill) {
      h += '<div style="background:#1a1a1a;border:1px solid #444;border-radius:8px;padding:10px;margin-top:6px">';
      h += '<div class="wiz-input-row">';
      h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Filter Depth</div>';
      h += '<select class="input-field" data-wiz-br-filterdepth="' + i + '">';
      ['1','2','4'].forEach(function(d){
        h += '<option value="' + d + '"' + ((br.filterDepth || '1') === d ? ' selected' : '') + '>' + d + '"</option>';
      });
      h += '</select></div>';
      h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">MERV Rating</div>';
      h += '<select class="input-field" data-wiz-br-grillmerv="' + i + '">';
      ['6','8','11','13'].forEach(function(m){
        h += '<option value="' + m + '"' + ((br.grillMerv || '8') === m ? ' selected' : '') + '>MERV ' + m + '</option>';
      });
      h += '</select></div>';
      h += '</div>';
      h += '<div class="wiz-input-row">';
      h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Grill Size</div>';
      h += '<select class="input-field" data-wiz-br-grillsize="' + i + '">';
      FILTER_GRILL_SIZES.forEach(function(s){
        h += '<option value="' + s + '"' + ((br.grillSize || '20x20') === s ? ' selected' : '') + '>' + s + '</option>';
      });
      h += '</select></div>';
      h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"></div>';
      h += '</div>';
      var fgPD = wizCalcFilterGrillPD(br);
      if (fgPD > 0) {
        var fgParts = (br.grillSize || '20x20').split('x');
        var fgW = parseFloat(fgParts[0]) || 20;
        var fgH = parseFloat(fgParts[1]) || 20;
        var fgArea = (fgW * fgH) / 144;
        var fgVel = fgArea > 0 ? (parseFloat(br.cfm) || 0) / fgArea : 0;
        var velColor = fgVel > 300 ? '#d32f2f' : fgVel > 200 ? '#ff9800' : '#4caf50';
        h += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:#888;margin-top:6px">Face vel: <span style="color:' + velColor + ';font-family:\'SF Mono\',monospace">' + Math.round(fgVel) + ' FPM</span> | PD: <span style="color:#ff9800;font-family:\'SF Mono\',monospace">' + fgPD.toFixed(3) + ' IWC</span></div>';
        if (fgVel > 300) {
          h += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:#d32f2f;margin-top:2px">Face velocity high — consider larger grill</div>';
        }
      }
      h += '</div>';
    }
  }

  // Runouts — sub-runs off this branch
  if (!br.runouts) br.runouts = [];
  if (br.runouts.length > 0) {
    h += '<div class="wiz-input-label" style="margin-top:8px;margin-bottom:4px;color:#ff9800">Runouts off this branch</div>';
    br.runouts.forEach(function(ro, ri) {
      var roFF = (ro.material === 'flex' && ro.compression) ? wizFlexFactor(ro.compression) : 1;
      h += '<div style="background:#1a1a1a;border:1px solid #444;border-radius:6px;padding:8px;margin-bottom:6px">';
      h += '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;margin-bottom:4px">';
      h += '<span style="font-size:11px;font-weight:600;color:#ff9800">Runout ' + (ri+1) + (ro.room ? ' \u2014 ' + ro.room : '') + '</span>';
      h += '<div data-wiz-rm-runout="' + i + '" data-ro-idx="' + ri + '" style="cursor:pointer;color:#888;font-size:16px;padding:2px 6px">\u00D7</div>';
      h += '</div>';
      h += '<div class="wiz-input-row">';
      h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Room</div><input type="text" class="input-field" value="' + (ro.room||'') + '" data-wiz-ro-room="' + i + '-' + ri + '"></div>';
      h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">CFM</div><input type="number" class="input-field" value="' + (ro.cfm||'') + '" placeholder="CFM" data-wiz-ro-cfm="' + i + '-' + ri + '"></div>';
      h += '</div>';
      h += '<div class="wiz-input-row">';
      h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Size</div><select class="input-field" data-wiz-ro-size="' + i + '-' + ri + '">';
      WIZ_ROUND_SIZES.forEach(function(s){ h += '<option value="'+s+'"'+(ro.size==s?' selected':'')+'>'+s+'\u2033</option>'; });
      h += '</select></div>';
      h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Length (ft)</div><input type="number" class="input-field" value="' + (ro.length||'6') + '" min="1" max="100" data-wiz-ro-len="' + i + '-' + ri + '"></div>';
      h += '</div>';
      h += '<div class="wiz-input-row">';
      h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Ends At</div><select class="input-field" data-wiz-ro-boot="' + i + '-' + ri + '">';
      Object.keys(WIZ_BOOT_EQ).forEach(function(k){ h += '<option value="'+k+'"'+(ro.bootType===k?' selected':'')+'>'+WIZ_BOOT_EQ[k].name+'</option>'; });
      h += '</select></div>';
      h += '<div class="wiz-input-group"><div class="wiz-input-label">Material</div><select class="input-field" data-wiz-ro-mat="' + i + '-' + ri + '">';
      h += '<option value="metal"' + (ro.material!=='flex'?' selected':'') + '>Metal</option>';
      h += '<option value="flex"' + (ro.material==='flex'?' selected':'') + '>Flex</option>';
      h += '</select></div>';
      h += '</div>';
      if (ro.material === 'flex') {
