var cfmSlider = document.getElementById('cfmSlider');
var cfmSliderVal = document.getElementById('cfmSliderVal');
if (cfmSlider && cfmSliderVal) {
  cfmSlider.addEventListener('input', function() {
    cfmSliderVal.value = cfmSlider.value;
    document.getElementById('cfmInput').value = cfmSlider.value;
    calculate();
  });
  cfmSliderVal.addEventListener('input', function() {
    var v = parseInt(cfmSliderVal.value) || 400;
    cfmSlider.value = Math.min(v, 2000);
    document.getElementById('cfmInput').value = v;
    calculate();
  });
}




// ===== FILTER INTEGRATION (Calc Tab + System Analyzer) =====

// Build filter HTML for system analyzer runs
function buildSysFilterHTML(r, runIdx) {
  if (r.airPath !== 'return') return '';
  var checked = r.hasFilter ? ' checked' : '';
  var configDisplay = r.hasFilter ? '' : ' style="display:none"';
  
  // Build model options for current mfg
  var models = FILTER_DB[r.filterMfg] || [];
  var modelOpts = models.map(function(m) {
    return '<option value="' + m.model + '"' + (m.model === r.filterModel ? ' selected' : '') + '>' + m.name + '</option>';
  }).join('');
  
  var grilleSizes = ['12x24','14x20','14x25','16x20','16x25','20x20','20x25','20x30','24x24','24x30','25x25'];
  var grilleOpts = grilleSizes.map(function(g) {
    return '<option value="' + g + '"' + (g === r.filterGrille ? ' selected' : '') + '>' + g + '</option>';
  }).join('');
  
  return '<div class="filter-inline-panel" style="margin-top:8px">' +
    '<div class="filter-toggle-row">' +
      '<svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--orange)" stroke-width="2" width="16" height="16"><rect x="3" y="3" width="18" height="18" rx="2"/><line x1="3" y1="9" x2="21" y2="9"/><line x1="3" y1="15" x2="21" y2="15"/><line x1="9" y1="3" x2="9" y2="21"/><line x1="15" y1="3" x2="15" y2="21"/></svg>' +
      '<span class="filter-toggle-label">Filter Grille on Return</span>' +
      '<label class="toggle-switch"><input type="checkbox" data-sys-filter-toggle="' + runIdx + '"' + checked + '><span class="toggle-slider"></span></label>' +
    '</div>' +
    '<div data-sys-filter-config="' + runIdx + '"' + configDisplay + '>' +
      '<div class="filter-select-row">' +
        '<div><label class="config-label">Manufacturer</label><select class="input-field" data-sys-filter-mfg="' + runIdx + '" style="width:100%">' +
          '<option value="aprilaire"' + (r.filterMfg==='aprilaire'?' selected':'') + '>Aprilaire</option>' +
          '<option value="honeywell"' + (r.filterMfg==='honeywell'?' selected':'') + '>Honeywell</option>' +
          '<option value="lennox"' + (r.filterMfg==='lennox'?' selected':'') + '>Lennox</option>' +
          '<option value="carrier"' + (r.filterMfg==='carrier'?' selected':'') + '>Carrier</option>' +
          '<option value="generic"' + (r.filterMfg==='generic'?' selected':'') + '>Generic</option>' +
        '</select></div>' +
        '<div><label class="config-label">Model / MERV</label><select class="input-field" data-sys-filter-model="' + runIdx + '" style="width:100%">' + modelOpts + '</select></div>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div class="filter-select-row" style="margin-top:6px">' +
        '<div><label class="config-label">Filter Grille Size</label><select class="input-field" data-sys-filter-grille="' + runIdx + '" style="width:100%">' + grilleOpts + '</select></div>' +
      '</div>' +
    '</div>' +
  '</div>';
}

// Calc tab filter: show/hide based on airPath
function updateCalcFilterVisibility() {
  var sec = document.getElementById('calcFilterSection');
  var disc = document.getElementById('calcFilterDisclaimer');
  if (sec) sec.style.display = state.airPath === 'return' ? '' : 'none';
  if (disc) disc.style.display = state.airPath === 'return' ? '' : 'none';
}

// Calc tab filter: populate models when mfg changes
function updateCalcFilterModels() {
  var mfgSel = document.getElementById('calcFilterMfg');
  var modelSel = document.getElementById('calcFilterModel');
  if (!mfgSel || !modelSel) return;
  var models = FILTER_DB[mfgSel.value] || [];
  modelSel.innerHTML = models.map(function(m) {
    return '<option value="' + m.model + '">' + m.name + '</option>';
  }).join('');
  calcCalcFilter();
}

// Calc tab filter: calculate and display results
function calcCalcFilter() {
  var toggle = document.getElementById('calcFilterToggle');
  var configDiv = document.getElementById('calcFilterConfig');
  var resultsDiv = document.getElementById('calcFilterResults');
  var warnDiv = document.getElementById('calcFilterWarn');
  if (!toggle || !configDiv) return;
  
  configDiv.style.display = toggle.checked ? '' : 'none';
  if (!toggle.checked) {
    if (resultsDiv) resultsDiv.innerHTML = '';
    if (warnDiv) { warnDiv.style.display = 'none'; warnDiv.innerHTML = ''; }
    return;
  }
  
  var mfg = document.getElementById('calcFilterMfg').value;
  var modelId = document.getElementById('calcFilterModel').value;
  var grille = document.getElementById('calcFilterGrille').value;
  var sysCFM = parseFloat(document.getElementById('calcFilterCFM').value) || 1200;
  
  var models = FILTER_DB[mfg] || [];
  var filt = models.find(function(m) { return m.model === modelId; });
  if (!filt) return;
  
  // Face velocity
  var gParts = grille.split('x');
  var gArea = (parseInt(gParts[0]) * parseInt(gParts[1])) / 144;
  var faceVel = sysCFM / gArea;
  
  // PD scaled by square law
  var ratio = sysCFM / filt.ratedCfm;
  var pd = filt.ratedPD * ratio * ratio;
  
  var fvClass = faceVel > 500 ? 'danger' : (faceVel > 400 ? 'warn' : 'ok');
  var pdClass = pd > 0.25 ? 'danger' : (pd > 0.15 ? 'warn' : 'ok');
  
  resultsDiv.innerHTML = 
    '<div class="filter-inline-stat"><div class="filter-inline-stat-val ' + fvClass + '">' + Math.round(faceVel) + '</div><div class="filter-inline-stat-label">Face Vel (FPM)</div></div>' +
    '<div class="filter-inline-stat"><div class="filter-inline-stat-val ' + pdClass + '">' + pd.toFixed(2) + '</div><div class="filter-inline-stat-label">Filter PD (IWC)</div></div>' +
    '<div class="filter-inline-stat"><div class="filter-inline-stat-val">' + filt.merv + '</div><div class="filter-inline-stat-label">MERV Rating</div></div>' +
    '<div class="filter-inline-stat"><div class="filter-inline-stat-val">' + filt.depth + '"</div><div class="filter-inline-stat-label">Filter Depth</div></div>';
  
  // Warnings
  var warns = [];
  if (faceVel > 500) warns.push('<strong>\u26a0 Face velocity ' + Math.round(faceVel) + ' FPM exceeds 500 FPM max.</strong> ASHRAE 52.2 standard test velocity is 492 FPM. Increase grille size or use two return grilles.');
  if (faceVel > 300 && faceVel <= 500) warns.push('Face velocity ' + Math.round(faceVel) + ' FPM is within ASHRAE test range (300\u2013492 FPM). Acceptable for filter grille applications.');
  if (pd > 0.30) warns.push('Filter pressure drop of ' + pd.toFixed(2) + ' IWC is very high. Consider a lower MERV or deeper filter media to reduce restriction.');
  
  if (warns.length > 0) {
    var warnClass = faceVel > 500 ? 'danger' : '';
    warnDiv.style.display = '';
    warnDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="filter-warning-banner ' + warnClass + '" style="margin-top:8px"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" width="14" height="14"><path d="M10.29 3.86L1.82 18a2 2 0 001.71 3h16.94a2 2 0 001.71-3L13.71 3.86a2 2 0 00-3.42 0z"/><line x1="12" y1="9" x2="12" y2="13"/><line x1="12" y1="17" x2="12.01" y2="17"/></svg><span>' + warns.join('<br>') + '</span></div>';
  } else {
    warnDiv.style.display = 'none';
  }
}

// Show/hide system analyzer filter disclaimer
function updateSysFilterDisclaimer() {
  var disc = document.getElementById('sysFilterDisclaimer');
  if (!disc) return;
  var hasReturn = SS.runs.some(function(r) { return r.airPath === 'return'; });
  disc.style.display = hasReturn ? '' : 'none';
}

var filterState = { mfg: 'aprilaire', model: null, pd: 0 };

function populateFilterModels(mfg) {
  filterState.mfg = mfg;
  var sel = document.getElementById('filterModel');
  if (!sel) return;
  var models = FILTER_DB[mfg] || [];
  sel.innerHTML = models.map(function(m) {
    return '<option value="' + m.model + '">' + m.name + ' (MERV ' + m.merv + ')</option>';
  }).join('');
  if (models.length > 0) {
    filterState.model = models[0].model;
  }
  calcFilterPD();
}

function calcFilterPD() {
  var models = FILTER_DB[filterState.mfg] || [];
  var sel = document.getElementById('filterModel');
  var modelId = sel ? sel.value : '';
  var filt = models.find(function(m){ return m.model === modelId; });
  if (!filt) {
    document.getElementById('filterPD').textContent = '--';
    document.getElementById('filterMERV').textContent = '--';
    document.getElementById('filterSize').textContent = '--';
    filterState.pd = 0;
    return;
  }

  var sysCfm = parseFloat(document.getElementById('filterCFM').value) || 1200;
  // Square-law scaling: PD_actual = PD_rated * (CFM_actual / CFM_rated)^2
  var ratio = sysCfm / filt.ratedCfm;
  var pd = filt.ratedPD * ratio * ratio;

  filterState.pd = pd;
  filterState.model = modelId;

  document.getElementById('filterPD').textContent = pd.toFixed(2);
  document.getElementById('filterMERV').textContent = filt.merv;
  document.getElementById('filterSize').textContent = filt.depth + '"';

  var noteEl = document.getElementById('filterNote');
  if (noteEl) {
    if (pd > 0.30) {
      noteEl.style.display = 'block';
      noteEl.textContent = '\u26a0 High pressure drop (' + pd.toFixed(2) + ' IWC). Consider a larger filter or lower MERV rating to avoid restricted airflow.';
    } else if (filt.note) {
      noteEl.style.display = 'block';
      noteEl.textContent = filt.note + ' \u2014 Rated: ' + filt.ratedPD.toFixed(2) + ' IWC @ ' + filt.ratedCfm + ' CFM. Scaled to ' + sysCfm + ' CFM.';
    } else {
      noteEl.style.display = 'none';
    }
  }
}

function applyFilterToFRWorksheet() {
  if (filterState.pd <= 0) return;
  // Apply to high/mid efficiency filter field in FR Worksheet
  var hiFilter = document.getElementById('frCPL_hiFilter');
  if (hiFilter) {
    hiFilter.value = filterState.pd.toFixed(2);
    calcFrictionRate();
    // Flash the input to show it was updated
    hiFilter.style.background = 'rgba(211,47,47,0.3)';
    setTimeout(function(){ hiFilter.style.background = ''; }, 1500);
  }
  // Also apply to low filter field if it has a value
  var loFilter = document.getElementById('frCPL_loFilter');
  // Switch to FR Worksheet tab
  showPage('frworksheet');
}

// Filter page event delegation
(function(){
  var filterPage = document.getElementById('page-filters');
  if (!filterPage) return;

  filterPage.addEventListener('click', function(ev) {
    var t = ev.target.closest('[data-filter-mfg]');
    if (t) {
      filterPage.querySelectorAll('[data-filter-mfg]').forEach(function(b){ b.classList.remove('active'); });
      t.classList.add('active');
      populateFilterModels(t.dataset.filterMfg);
      return;
    }
    if (ev.target.closest('#filterApplyBtn')) {
      applyFilterToFRWorksheet();
      return;
    }
  });

  filterPage.addEventListener('change', function(ev) {
    if (ev.target.id === 'filterModel') calcFilterPD();
  });

  filterPage.addEventListener('input', function(ev) {
    if (ev.target.id === 'filterCFM') calcFilterPD();
  });

  // Init
  populateFilterModels('aprilaire');
})();

// Init calc tab filter (must be after FILTER_DB)
updateCalcFilterModels();

// Init return plenum filter
initSysRetFilterModels();
document.getElementById('sysRetFilterToggle').addEventListener('change', function() {
  calcSysRetFilter();
  calcSystem();
});
document.getElementById('sysRetFilterMfg').addEventListener('change', function() {
  sysRetFilterState.mfg = this.value;
  initSysRetFilterModels();
});
document.getElementById('sysRetFilterModel').addEventListener('change', function() {
  sysRetFilterState.model = this.value;
  calcSysRetFilter();
  calcSystem();
});
document.getElementById('sysRetFilterGrille').addEventListener('change', function() {
  calcSysRetFilter();
  calcSystem();
});
document.getElementById('sysRetFilterCFM').addEventListener('input', function() {
  calcSysRetFilter();
});

// ===== ROOM CFM CALCULATOR =====
const ROOM_CFM_TYPES = [
  {id:'master_bed', label:'Master Bedroom', cfmPerSqft:0.75, minCfm:100, maxCfm:400, achNote:'0.7-0.8 CFM/ft²'},

  {id:'living', label:'Living Room', cfmPerSqft:1.0, minCfm:200, maxCfm:600, achNote:'1.0 CFM/ft², 6-8 ACH'},
  {id:'great_room', label:'Great Room', cfmPerSqft:1.0, minCfm:250, maxCfm:800, achNote:'1.0 CFM/ft², 6-8 ACH'},
  {id:'kitchen', label:'Kitchen', cfmPerSqft:1.2, minCfm:150, maxCfm:500, achNote:'1.2 CFM/ft², higher load'},
  {id:'dining', label:'Dining Room', cfmPerSqft:0.9, minCfm:100, maxCfm:400, achNote:'0.9 CFM/ft²'},
  {id:'master_bath', label:'Master Bathroom', cfmPerSqft:1.0, minCfm:50, maxCfm:200, achNote:'50-80 CFM typical'},
  {id:'bathroom', label:'Bathroom', cfmPerSqft:1.0, minCfm:50, maxCfm:150, achNote:'50-80 CFM typical'},
  {id:'laundry', label:'Laundry Room', cfmPerSqft:1.0, minCfm:80, maxCfm:250, achNote:'Higher load'},
  {id:'office', label:'Office/Study', cfmPerSqft:0.8, minCfm:80, maxCfm:300, achNote:'0.8 CFM/ft²'},
  {id:'hallway', label:'Hallway', cfmPerSqft:0.5, minCfm:25, maxCfm:150, achNote:'0.5 CFM/ft²'},
  {id:'garage', label:'Garage (conditioned)', cfmPerSqft:0.5, minCfm:0, maxCfm:400, achNote:'If conditioned'},
  {id:'bonus', label:'Bonus Room', cfmPerSqft:0.9, minCfm:100, maxCfm:500, achNote:'0.9 CFM/ft²'},
  {id:'closet', label:'Walk-in Closet', cfmPerSqft:0.5, minCfm:15, maxCfm:100, achNote:'Minimal'},
];

let roomCfmData = [
  {name:'Master Bedroom', type:'master_bed', length:14, width:12, ceilHt:8},
  {name:'Master Bath', type:'master_bath', length:10, width:8, ceilHt:8},
  {name:'Bedroom 2', type:'bedroom', length:12, width:10, ceilHt:8},
  {name:'Bedroom 3', type:'bedroom', length:11, width:10, ceilHt:8},
  {name:'Living Room', type:'living', length:18, width:14, ceilHt:8},
  {name:'Kitchen', type:'kitchen', length:14, width:12, ceilHt:8},
  {name:'Bathroom', type:'bathroom', length:8, width:6, ceilHt:8},
];
let roomCfmTightness = 'semi-tight';

function calcRoomCfm(room) {
  var rt = ROOM_CFM_TYPES.find(function(t){return t.id===room.type;}) || ROOM_CFM_TYPES[1];
  var ht = HOUSE_TIGHTNESS.find(function(h){return h.id===roomCfmTightness;}) || HOUSE_TIGHTNESS[1];
  var sqft = room.length * room.width;
  var vol = sqft * (room.ceilHt || 8);
  
  // Tightness multiplier: tight houses need less CFM, loose need more
  // Baseline is semi-tight (1.0x), tight=0.85, average=1.15, semi-loose=1.3, loose=1.5
  var tightMult = {'tight':0.85, 'semi-tight':1.0, 'average':1.15, 'semi-loose':1.3, 'loose':1.5};
  var mult = tightMult[roomCfmTightness] || 1.0;
  
  // Calculate CFM based on sqft and room type rate
  var cfm = sqft * rt.cfmPerSqft * mult;
  // Clamp to min/max for room type (max scales with tightness for oversized rooms)
  cfm = Math.max(rt.minCfm, Math.min(rt.maxCfm * mult, cfm));
  
  return {cfm: Math.round(cfm), sqft: sqft, vol: vol, rt: rt};
}

var _roomCardCount = 0;

function renderRoomCfm(fullRebuild) {
  var c = document.getElementById('roomCfmList');
  if (!c) return;
  
  var needsRebuild = fullRebuild || (_roomCardCount !== roomCfmData.length);
  var totalCfm = 0, totalSqft = 0, totalVol = 0;
  
  if (needsRebuild) {
    var typeOpts = ROOM_CFM_TYPES.map(function(t){return '<option value="'+t.id+'">'+t.label+'</option>';}).join('');
    c.innerHTML = roomCfmData.map(function(rm, i) {
      var calc = calcRoomCfm(rm);
      totalCfm += calc.cfm;
      totalSqft += calc.sqft;
      totalVol += calc.vol;
      return '<div class="room-card" data-room-idx="'+i+'">' +
        '<div class="room-card-header">' +
          '<button class="room-card-remove" data-room-rm="'+i+'">&times;</button>' +
          '<input type="text" class="room-card-name" value="'+rm.name+'" data-room-name="'+i+'">' +
          '<div class="room-card-cfm" data-room-cfm-out="'+i+'">'+calc.cfm+'<span class="room-card-cfm-unit"> CFM</span></div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="room-card-body">' +
          '<div class="room-input-group">' +
            '<span class="room-input-label">Length (ft)</span>' +
            '<input type="number" class="room-input-field" value="'+rm.length+'" data-room-len="'+i+'" min="1" max="100" step="0.5">' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="room-input-group">' +
            '<span class="room-input-label">Width (ft)</span>' +
            '<input type="number" class="room-input-field" value="'+rm.width+'" data-room-wid="'+i+'" min="1" max="100" step="0.5">' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="room-input-group">' +
            '<span class="room-input-label">Ceiling (ft)</span>' +
            '<input type="number" class="room-input-field" value="'+(rm.ceilHt||8)+'" data-room-ht="'+i+'" min="6" max="20" step="0.5">' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="room-input-group">' +
            '<span class="room-input-label">Type</span>' +
            '<select class="room-type-select" data-room-type="'+i+'" style="grid-column:auto">'+typeOpts.replace('value="'+rm.type+'"','value="'+rm.type+'" selected')+'</select>' +
          '</div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="room-card-info" data-room-info-out="'+i+'">' +
          '<span>'+calc.sqft+' ft\u00b2 \u00b7 '+calc.vol+' ft\u00b3</span>' +
          '<span>'+calc.rt.achNote+'</span>' +
        '</div>' +
      '</div>';
    }).join('');
    _roomCardCount = roomCfmData.length;
  } else {
    // In-place update: only update calculated outputs, NOT input elements
    // This preserves focus and keyboard on iOS
    roomCfmData.forEach(function(rm, i) {
      var calc = calcRoomCfm(rm);
      totalCfm += calc.cfm;
      totalSqft += calc.sqft;
      totalVol += calc.vol;
      var cfmEl = document.querySelector('[data-room-cfm-out="'+i+'"]');
      if (cfmEl) cfmEl.innerHTML = calc.cfm + '<span class="room-card-cfm-unit"> CFM</span>';
      var infoEl = document.querySelector('[data-room-info-out="'+i+'"]');
      if (infoEl) infoEl.innerHTML = '<span>'+calc.sqft+' ft\u00b2 \u00b7 '+calc.vol+' ft\u00b3</span><span>'+calc.rt.achNote+'</span>';
    });
  }
  
  var e = function(id){return document.getElementById(id);};
  if(e('roomTotalCfm')) e('roomTotalCfm').textContent = totalCfm;
  if(e('roomTotalTons')) e('roomTotalTons').textContent = (totalCfm / 400).toFixed(1);
  if(e('roomTotalSqft')) e('roomTotalSqft').textContent = totalSqft;
  if(e('roomTotalVol')) e('roomTotalVol').textContent = totalVol;
  
  var ts = document.getElementById('roomTightnessSelect');
  if (ts) {
    ts.innerHTML = HOUSE_TIGHTNESS.map(function(h) {
      return '<button class="tightness-btn'+(h.id===roomCfmTightness?' active':'')+'\" data-room-tightness="'+h.id+'"><div class="tightness-btn-label">'+h.label+'</div><div class="tightness-btn-ach">H:'+h.hACH+' / C:'+h.cACH+'</div></button>';
    }).join('');
  }
  var td = document.getElementById('roomTightnessDesc');
  var ht = HOUSE_TIGHTNESS.find(function(h){return h.id===roomCfmTightness;}) || HOUSE_TIGHTNESS[1];
  if (td) td.textContent = ht.desc;
}

// Room CFM event delegation
document.getElementById('page-roomcfm').addEventListener('click', function(ev) {
  var t = ev.target;
  var rm = t.closest('[data-room-rm]');
  if (rm) { roomCfmData.splice(parseInt(rm.dataset.roomRm), 1); renderRoomCfm(true); return; }
  
  var tb = t.closest('[data-room-tightness]');
  if (tb) { roomCfmTightness = tb.dataset.roomTightness; renderRoomCfm(true); return; }
  
  if (t.closest('#roomAddBtn')) {
    roomCfmData.push({name:'Room '+(roomCfmData.length+1), type:'bedroom', length:12, width:10, ceilHt:8});
    renderRoomCfm(true);
    return;
  }
});
document.getElementById('page-roomcfm').addEventListener('input', function(ev) {
  var t = ev.target;
  if (t.dataset.roomName !== undefined) { roomCfmData[parseInt(t.dataset.roomName)].name = t.value; return; }
  if (t.dataset.roomLen !== undefined) { roomCfmData[parseInt(t.dataset.roomLen)].length = parseFloat(t.value)||0; renderRoomCfm(); return; }
  if (t.dataset.roomWid !== undefined) { roomCfmData[parseInt(t.dataset.roomWid)].width = parseFloat(t.value)||0; renderRoomCfm(); return; }
  if (t.dataset.roomHt !== undefined) { roomCfmData[parseInt(t.dataset.roomHt)].ceilHt = parseFloat(t.value)||8; renderRoomCfm(); return; }
});
document.getElementById('page-roomcfm').addEventListener('change', function(ev) {
  var t = ev.target;
  if (t.dataset.roomType !== undefined) { roomCfmData[parseInt(t.dataset.roomType)].type = t.value; renderRoomCfm(true); return; }
});


renderRoomCfm();
psychCalc();

calcFrictionRate();
</script>
